🎯 MVP Roles for Indian Education System (NOVAA/Smart College)\n\n> **Scope**: Core 15 roles for Phase 1 launch — covers 90% of daily operations for schools/colleges in India\n\n---\n\n## 🏛️ Platform Level (SaaS Multi-Tenant)\n\n| Role | Description |\n|------|-------------|\n| **SUPER_ADMIN** | Platform-wide owner; manages college onboarding, subscriptions, global settings, system audits, and DPDPA compliance oversight. |\n| **PLATFORM_SUPPORT** | Technical support role; troubleshoots tenant issues, manages backups, handles escalation without accessing sensitive academic/financial data. |\n\n---\n\n## 🎓 College Administration\n\n| Role | Description |\n|------|-------------|\n| **COLLEGE_ADMIN** | Institution owner/manager; full CRUD access to students, staff, departments, fees, and reports within their college tenant only. |\n| **PRINCIPAL** | Academic head; oversees curriculum, approvals, delegations, strategic reports; read-mostly with selective write permissions. |\n| **ACCOUNTANT** | Manages fee collection, payment tracking, receipts, financial reports; no access to academic performance data. |\n| **ADMISSION_OFFICER** | Handles application intake, document verification, counseling, enrollment; access limited to pending applications only. |\n| **EXAM_COORDINATOR** | Manages exam schedules, hall tickets, invigilation, result processing; cross-department read access for student/teacher lists. |\n| **HOD** *(Head of Department)* | Department-level academic lead; approves leaves, views dept students/staff, manages curriculum delivery within own department. |\n\n---\n\n## 👨‍🏫 Academic Delivery\n\n| Role | Description |\n|------|-------------|\n| **TEACHER** | Delivers instruction; marks attendance, uploads assignments, views class students, creates notifications; scoped to assigned classes/departments. |\n| **TUTOR / MENTOR** | Student welfare role; tracks assigned mentees' attendance, performance, grievances; limited academic data access for counseling. |\n\n---\n\n## 👨‍🎓 Student & Guardian Experience\n\n| Role | Description |\n|------|-------------|\n| **STUDENT** | Primary end-user; views own timetable, attendance, fees, results, assignments; submits work, downloads receipts, updates profile. |\n| **PARENT_GUARDIAN** | Linked to student(s); views child's attendance, fees, results, notices; receives alerts; no edit permissions. |\n| **PROSPECTIVE_APPLICANT** | Pre-enrollment role; submits application, uploads documents, tracks status, pays admission fee; data purged if not enrolled (DPDPA). |\n\n---\n\n## 🏥 Essential Support Roles\n\n| Role | Description |\n|------|-------------|\n| **LIBRARIAN** | Manages book inventory, issuance/returns, fines; integrates with student records for eligibility checks. |\n| **PLACEMENT_OFFICER** | Manages student placements, company drives, interviews, offers; accesses final-year student profiles and academic summaries. |\n\n---\n\n## 🔐 MVP Permission Boundaries (Quick Reference)\n\n```\n✅ COLLEGE_ADMIN: Can do everything within college tenant\n✅ PRINCIPAL: Can read all, write academic/HR, delegate selectively\n✅ ACCOUNTANT: Financial data only; no academic records\n✅ ADMISSION_OFFICER: Pending applications only; auto-expire post-cycle\n✅ EXAM_COORDINATOR: Exam workflow only; results require Principal approval\n✅ HOD: Department-scoped; cannot cross dept boundaries\n✅ TEACHER: Class/subject-scoped; cannot view unrelated student data\n✅ STUDENT/PARENT: Own data only; read-mostly\n✅ PROSPECTIVE_APPLICANT: Application flow only; GDPR/DPDPA-compliant purge\n```\n\n---\n\n## 🇮🇳 India-Specific MVP Considerations\n\n| Feature | Why It Matters for India |\n|---------|-------------------------|\n| **Multi-language UI** | Support Hindi + regional languages for student/parent roles |\n| **Aadhaar/UID integration** | Optional for admission/verification workflows |\n| **Scholarship tracking** | SC/ST/OBC/EWS categories in student profiles; ACCOUNTANT handles disbursement |\n| **Academic year flexibility** | Support June-July start (not Jan-Dec); EXAM_COORDINATOR manages term cycles |\n| **Fee installment logic** | ACCOUNTANT handles partial payments, late fines, waiver approvals |\n| **DPDPA consent logging** | All roles: explicit consent capture for data collection, especially ADMISSION_OFFICER |\n| **Affiliation board support** | PRINCIPAL/COLLEGE_ADMIN manage CBSE/State Board/University curriculum variants |\n\n---\n\n## 🚀 MVP Role Implementation Order\n\n1. `COLLEGE_ADMIN` → Foundation tenant setup\n2. `STUDENT` + `TEACHER` → Core academic loop\n3. `ACCOUNTANT` → Revenue enablement (critical for Indian colleges)\n4. `ADMISSION_OFFICER` → Student intake pipeline\n5. `PRINCIPAL` + `HOD` → Approval workflows & hierarchy\n6. `PARENT_GUARDIAN` → Engagement & retention\n7. `EXAM_COORDINATOR` → Assessment cycle\n8. `SUPER_ADMIN` + `PLATFORM_SUPPORT` → SaaS operations\n9. `LIBRARIAN` + `PLACEMENT_OFFICER` → Value-add modules\n10. `PROSPECTIVE_APPLICANT` + `TUTOR` → Edge cases & welfare\n\n---\n\n> 💡 **Pro Tip**: Start with just **8 core roles** for alpha launch:  \n> `SUPER_ADMIN`, `COLLEGE_ADMIN`, `TEACHER`, `STUDENT`, `ACCOUNTANT`, `PRINCIPAL`, `PARENT_GUARDIAN`, `ADMISSION_OFFICER`  \n> Add the rest in Phase 1.1 based on pilot college feedback.\n\nNeed me to draft the permission seed script for these 15 MVP roles next? Below is a prioritized action plan mapped to your MVP scope, hybrid permission model, and Indian compliance requirements.\n\n---\n\n## 📊 Prioritized Action Matrix\n\n| Module | Priority | Phase | Key Action | Business Impact |\n|--------|----------|-------|------------|-----------------|\n| 🔴 Subscription Expiry | Critical | V1.0 | Add missing fields, fix middleware, build admin UI | **Blocks SaaS billing & tenant lifecycle** |\n| 🔴 Soft Delete Restore Bug | Critical | V1.0 | Merge hooks, preserve original statuses, add snapshot | Prevents data corruption on tenant reactivation |\n| 🔴 Offline Subscription Expiry (Fix Immediately)\n```javascript\n// Add to College model\n{\n  plan: { type: String, enum: [\"TRIAL\", \"BASIC\", \"PREMIUM\"], default: \"TRIAL\" },\n  subscriptionExpiry: Date,\n  isTrial: Boolean,\n  gracePeriodEnd: Date // +7 days for warning banner\n}\n```\n- Update `collegeIsolation.middleware.js` to check actual fields\n- Add banner UI for colleges within 7 days of expiry\n- Build Super Admin subscription management UI\n\n### 🔴 2. Soft Delete / Cascade (Refactor)\nReplace dual hooks with a single state-machine hook:\n```javascript\ncollegeSchema.pre('findOneAndUpdate', async function(next) {\n  const update = this.getUpdate();\n  if (update.isActive === false && this._update.$set.isActive === false) {\n    // Deactivate: cascade to 14 collections, set isActive: false\n  } else if (update.isActive === true) {\n    // Restore: use pre-deletion snapshot or restore original statuses\n    // DO NOT blindly set students to APPROVED\n  }\n  next();\n});\n```\n**Recommendation**: Store pre-deletion state in a `CollegeDeactivationAudit` collection instead of toggling blindly.\n\n### 🔴 3. Offline Payment Receipts\n- Reuse your existing PDF generator\n- Trigger on `StudentFee.updateOne({ \"installments.paymentMode\": { $in: [\"CASH\",\"CHEQUE\",\"DD\"] } })`\n- Email receipt to student + college admin\n- Add `receiptUrl` field to installment schema\n\n### 🔴 4. Stripe Gateway\n- **Action**: Comment out Stripe routes, hide from admin UI\n- Keep encryption & webhook patterns for future NRI/international expansion\n- Document: `\"Razorpay is primary for India MVP (UPI, net banking, domestic cards). Stripe reserved for V2 international/NRI support.\"`\n\n### 🟡 5. Timetable Exception Notifications\n```javascript\n// After exception status → APPROVED\nconst affected = await getAffectedUsers(exception); // teachers, students, rooms\nawait Notification.create({\n  type: \"ACADEMIC\",\n  targetType: \"INDIVIDUAL\",\n  actionUrl: `/timetable/exceptions/${exception._id}`,\n  // trigger email service for teachers/students\n});\n```\n\n### 🟡 6. Installment Due Date Enforcement\n- Add `lateFee` field to `FeeStructure.installments[]`\n- Middleware: If `installment[2].status === \"PENDING\"` and user tries to pay `installment[3]`, return warning (or block based on college config)\n- Verify cron: `checkInstallmentDueDates()` should query `StudentFee` where `installments.dueDate < today && status === \"PENDING\"`\n\n### 🟡 7. HOD Permission Expansion (Hybrid Model)\nIn your permission seed script:\n```javascript\n{\n  role: \"HOD\",\n  permissions: [\n    { resource: \"timetables\", actions: [\"create\",\"read\",\"update\"], scope: \"own_department\" },\n    { resource: \"leave_requests\", actions: [\"approve\",\"read\"], scope: \"own_department\" },\n    { resource: \"department_reports\", actions: [\"read\",\"export\"], scope: \"own_department\" },\n    { resource: \"timetable_exceptions\", actions: [\"approve\"], scope: \"own_department\" }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n### 🟡 8. Notification Routing & Expiry\n- Frontend: `actionUrl` → React Router dynamic redirect\n- Backend cron: `Notification.updateMany({ expiresAt: { $lt: new Date() }, isExpired: false }, { $set: { isExpired: true } })`\n- Email trigger: Only for `URGENT`, `FEE`, `EXAM` types to avoid spam\n\n### 🟢 9. Timetable Module\n\nWhat's actually built:\n\n    Timetable\n\n    — one per department/course/semester/academic year, has DRAFT → PUBLISHED → ARCHIVED lifecycle, date range with working days, IST timezone\n\n    TimetableSlot\n\n    — individual class slots (day, startTime, endTime, subject, teacher, room, LECTURE/LAB type)\n\n    TimetableException\n\n    — 8 exception types: HOLIDAY, CANCELLED, EXTRA, RESCHEDULED, ROOM_CHANGE, TEACHER_CHANGE, SPECIAL_EVENT, EXAM. Has full approval workflow (PENDING → APPROVED/REJECTED), recurring patterns, substitute teacher support\n\n    HOD middleware — only the HOD of a department can create/manage timetables for that department\n\n    Student timetable view, teacher schedule view, weekly timetable UI\n\nMaturity: This is a fully thought-out, production-grade module. The exception model alone is more sophisticated than most commercial college systems. The slot snapshot in attendance sessions (preserving timetable state at time of session) is a smart design decision.\n\nGap: Exception notifications are modelled (\n\nnotifyAffected\n\n,\n\nnotificationsSent\n\nfields) but the actual notification sending when an exception is approved is not wired up.\n2. Teacher Attendance\n\nWhat's actually built:\n\n    teacherAttendance.controller.js\n\n    — generates a report of all closed sessions a teacher conducted, with present/absent counts and percentage per lecture\n\n    This is a teacher's own teaching record, not a separate attendance system for tracking whether teachers showed up\n\nWhat it is NOT:\n\n    There is no system to track whether a teacher was present or absent on a given day\n\n    No admin view of teacher attendance\n\n    No teacher attendance marking by admin or principal\n\nMaturity: Partial. What exists is a teacher's lecture delivery report, not teacher attendance management. The naming is misleading — it should be called \"Teacher Lecture Report.\"\n\nGap: If colleges need to track teacher presence (which they do for salary, NAAC), this needs a separate model and workflow.\n3. Student Promotion / Alumni\n\nWhat's actually built:\n\n    PromotionHistory\n\n    model — tracks fromSemester → toSemester, fromAcademicYear → toAcademicYear, fee status at time of promotion, who promoted, remarks, reversible\n\n    promoteStudent\n\n    and\n\n    bulkPromoteStudents\n\n    — admin can promote individual or bulk students\n\n    getPromotionEligibleStudents\n\n    — filters APPROVED students, shows fee status\n\n    isFinalSemesterPromotion\n\n    flag — when student completes final semester, status moves to ALUMNI\n\n    Student model has\n\n    currentSemester\n\n    ,\n\n    currentYear\n\n    (auto-calculated),\n\n    currentAcademicYear\n\n    ,\n\n    isPromotionEligible\n\n    ,\n\n    promotionHistory[]\n\nMaturity: Solid. The fee status check at promotion time (FULLY_PAID / PARTIALLY_PAID / PENDING) is a real business requirement — colleges won't promote students with pending fees. The reversal capability is also well thought out.\n\nGap: No email/notification sent to student when promoted. No bulk promotion with fee override (e.g., promote despite pending fees with admin justification).\n4. Installment-Based Payments\n\nWhat's actually built:\n\n    FeeStructure\n\n    — defined per college + course + category (GEN/OBC/SC/ST/EWS), has\n\n    installments[]\n\n    array with name, amount, dueDate\n\n    StudentFee\n\n    — per student, mirrors the fee structure installments, tracks status (PENDING/PAID/FAILED/CANCELLED) per installment, paidAmount vs totalFee\n\n    Atomic update on payment — uses\n\n    updateOne\n\n    with\n\n    status: \"PENDING\"\n\n    condition to prevent race conditions\n\n    Duplicate payment protection at two layers (status check + paymentId check)\n\nMaturity: Very solid. The category-based fee structure (different fees for SC/ST vs GEN) is a real Indian college requirement. The atomic update pattern is correct.\n\nGap: No due date enforcement — a student can pay installment 2 before installment 1. No late payment penalty logic. No installment due date reminder (the cron exists but needs to be verified it checks per-installment due dates).\n5. Offline Payment Recording\n\nWhat's actually built:\n\n    StudentFee.installments\n\n    has\n\n    paymentMode\n\n    (ONLINE/CASH/CHEQUE/DD),\n\n    referenceNumber\n\n    (for cheque/DD),\n\n    remarks\n\n    ,\n\n    markedByAdmin\n\n    Admin can mark an installment as paid offline with mode, reference number, and remarks\n\n    Full audit trail — which admin marked it, when\n\nMaturity: Complete and well-designed. This is critical for Indian colleges where many students still pay by cash or DD at the counter.\n\nGap: No receipt generation for offline payments. Online payments generate a PDF receipt via email — offline payments should too.\n6. Stripe Gateway\n\nWhat's actually built:\n\n    Full Stripe integration parallel to Razorpay\n\n    CollegePaymentConfig\n\n    — each college configures their own gateway (stripe or razorpay), credentials stored encrypted using AES-256-GCM\n\n    Per-college gateway instances cached in memory (5min TTL)\n\n    Stripe webhook handler\n\n    College admin UI to configure Stripe keys\n\nMaturity: The architecture is good — per-college payment credentials with encryption is the right approach. The encryption uses PBKDF2 key derivation which is solid.\n\nGap: Having both Stripe and Razorpay creates confusion. Razorpay is the right choice for India (UPI, Indian cards, net banking). Stripe is primarily for international cards. For MVP targeting Maharashtra colleges, Stripe adds complexity with no benefit. Decision needed: keep both but document when to use which, or deprecate Stripe for V1.\n7. Configurable Document Requirements\n\nWhat's actually built:\n\n    DocumentConfig\n\n    — per college, per\n\n    collegeCode\n\n    , list of document types each with: enabled/disabled toggle, mandatory flag, allowed formats, max file size (1-20MB), description, display order\n\n    18 document types supported: 10th marksheet, 12th marksheet, passport photo, category certificate, income certificate, character certificate, transfer certificate, Aadhaar, entrance exam score, migration certificate, domicile certificate, caste certificate, non-creamy layer, physically challenged, sports quota, NRI sponsor, gap certificate, affidavit\n\n    Student registration dynamically validates against the college's config\n\n    Category certificate skipped automatically if student is GEN category\n\nMaturity: This is genuinely impressive. Most college systems hardcode document requirements. This is fully configurable per college, which is exactly what's needed for Maharashtra's varied institution types (arts, science, engineering, medical all have different requirements).\n\nGap: No UI for admin to configure document requirements (the\n\nDocumentSettings.jsx\n\npage exists in frontend but needs verification it's fully wired). No version history — if a college changes document config mid-admission season, students who already submitted may be affected.\n8. HOD Role\n\nWhat's actually built:\n\n    HOD is a teacher with elevated timetable permissions, not a separate role in the ROLE enum\n\n    Department\n\n    model has\n\n    hod_id\n\n    field pointing to a Teacher\n\n    hod.middleware.js\n\n    — checks if the requesting teacher is the HOD of the department that owns the timetable\n\n    HOD can create, edit, publish timetables and manage slots for their department only\n\n    AssignHod.jsx\n\n    — admin UI to assign a teacher as HOD\n\nMaturity: Clean design — HOD is a permission layer on top of TEACHER, not a separate role. This avoids role explosion.\n\nGap: HOD has no other elevated permissions beyond timetable management. In reality, HODs also approve leave, manage department reports, approve timetable exceptions. The exception approval workflow exists in the model but it's not clear if HOD is the approver or admin.\n9. Notification System\n\nWhat's actually built:\n\n    Notification\n\n    model — college-scoped, created by COLLEGE_ADMIN or TEACHER\n\n    8 notification types: GENERAL, ACADEMIC, EXAM, FEE, ATTENDANCE, EVENT, ASSIGNMENT, URGENT\n\n    7 targeting options: ALL, STUDENTS, TEACHERS, DEPARTMENT, COURSE, SEMESTER, INDIVIDUAL\n\n    NotificationRead\n\n    — separate model tracking read status per user (not a field on notification itself — correct design for broadcast notifications)\n\n    Unread count API per role\n\n    Admin and teacher can create, update, delete notifications\n\nMaturity: Well-designed. The separate read-tracking model is the right approach for broadcast notifications (avoids storing one record per user per notification). Granular targeting (by department, course, semester) is a real need.\n\nGap: Notifications are in-app only — no push notifications, no email trigger from notification creation. The\n\nactionUrl\n\nfield exists but no frontend routing based on it. No notification expiry enforcement (the\n\nexpiresAt\n\nfield exists but nothing checks it).\n10. Subscription Expiry on Colleges\n\nWhat's actually built:\n\n    collegeIsolation.middleware.js\n\n    checks\n\n    college.subscriptionExpiry\n\n    — if past expiry, blocks all requests with\n\n    SUBSCRIPTION_EXPIRED\n\n    error\n\n    Warns in logs if expiry is within 7 days\n\n    The\n\n    College\n\n    model does NOT have a\n\n    subscriptionExpiry\n\n    field — it's checked in middleware but never stored\n\nMaturity: Half-built. The enforcement logic exists in middleware but the data model doesn't support it. The\n\nCollege\n\nmodel has no\n\nsubscriptionExpiry\n\n,\n\nplan\n\n, or\n\nbillingCycle\n\nfields. So currently this check never triggers because the field is always undefined.\n\nGap: This is a critical business feature (SaaS billing) that's been started but not completed. Need to add\n\nsubscriptionExpiry\n\n,\n\nplan\n\n(TRIAL/BASIC/PREMIUM),\n\ntrialEndsAt\n\nto the College model, and a Super Admin UI to manage subscriptions.\n11. Soft Delete / Cascade Deactivation\n\nWhat's actually built:\n\n    College\n\n    model has two\n\n    pre('findOneAndUpdate')\n\n    hooks — one for soft delete (isActive → false cascades to all 14 related collections), one for restore (isActive → true restores all)\n\n    Also has\n\n    pre('findOneAndDelete')\n\n    for hard delete that removes all related data\n\n    Student deactivation (DEACTIVATED status) — separate from college deactivation\n\n    Teacher deactivation (\n\n    status: INACTIVE\n\n    )\n\n    User deactivation (\n\n    isActive: false\n\n    )\n\nMaturity: The cascade logic is thorough — covers departments, courses, students, teachers, subjects, fee structures, student fees, notifications, timetables, slots, attendance sessions, records, document configs, users. This is production-grade.\n\nGap: Two\n\npre('findOneAndUpdate')\n\nhooks on the same model for opposite operations is fragile — both hooks run on every\n\nfindOneAndUpdate\n\ncall, each checking their own condition. If both\n\nisActive: true\n\nand\n\nisActive: false\n\nare somehow in the same update (edge case), both hooks fire. Should be merged into one hook with an if/else. Also, the restore hook blindly sets all students back to APPROVED — students who were REJECTED or PENDING before the college was deactivated will incorrectly become APPROVED on restore.\nSummary for Stripe is primarily for international cards. For MVP targeting Maharashtra colleges, Stripe adds complexity with no benefit. Decision needed: keep both but document when to use which, or deprecate Stripe for V1.\n7. Configurable Document Requirements\n\nWhat's actually built:\n\n    DocumentConfig\n\n    — per college, per\n\n    collegeCode\n\n    , list of document types each with: enabled/disabled toggle, mandatory flag, allowed formats, max file size (1-20MB), description, display order\n\n    18 document types supported: 10th marksheet, 12th marksheet, passport photo, category certificate, income certificate, character certificate, transfer certificate, Aadhaar, entrance exam score, migration certificate, domicile certificate, caste certificate, non-creamy layer, physically challenged, sports quota, NRI sponsor, gap certificate, affidavit\n\n    Student registration dynamically validates against the college's config\n\n    Category certificate skipped automatically if student is GEN category\n\nMaturity: This is genuinely impressive. Most college systems hardcode document requirements. This is fully configurable per college, which is exactly what's needed for Maharashtra's varied institution types (arts, science, engineering, medical all have different requirements).\n\nGap: No UI for admin to configure document requirements (the\n\nDocumentSettings.jsx\n\npage exists in frontend but needs verification it's fully wired). No version history — if a college changes document config mid-admission season, students who already submitted may be affected.\n8. HOD Role\n\nWhat's actually built:\n\n    HOD is a teacher with elevated timetable permissions, not a separate role in the ROLE enum\n\n    Department\n\n    model has\n\n    hod_id\n\n    field pointing to a Teacher\n\n    hod.middleware.js\n\n    — checks if the requesting teacher is the HOD of the department that owns the timetable\n\n    HOD can create, edit, publish timetables and manage slots for their department only\n\n    AssignHod.jsx\n\n    — admin UI to assign a teacher as HOD\n\nMaturity: Clean design — HOD is a permission layer on top of TEACHER, not a separate role. This avoids role explosion.\n\nGap: HOD has no other elevated permissions beyond timetable management. In reality, HODs also approve leave, manage department reports, approve timetable exceptions. The exception approval workflow exists in the model but it's not clear if HOD is the approver or admin.\n9. Notification System\n\nWhat's actually built:\n\n    Notification\n\n    model — college-scoped, created by COLLEGE_ADMIN or TEACHER\n\n    8 notification types: GENERAL, ACADEMIC, EXAM, FEE, ATTENDANCE, EVENT, ASSIGNMENT, URGENT\n\n    7 targeting options: ALL, STUDENTS, TEACHERS, DEPARTMENT, COURSE, SEMESTER, INDIVIDUAL\n\n    NotificationRead\n\n    — separate model tracking read status per user (not a field on notification itself — correct design for broadcast notifications)\n\n    Unread count API per role\n\n    Admin and teacher can create, update, delete notifications\n\nMaturity: Well-designed. The separate read-tracking model is the right approach for broadcast notifications (avoids storing one record per user per notification). Granular targeting (by department, course, semester) is a real need.\n\nGap: Notifications are in-app only — no push notifications, no email trigger from notification creation. The\n\nactionUrl\n\nfield exists but no frontend routing based on it. No notification expiry enforcement (the\n\nexpiresAt\n\nfield exists but nothing checks it).\n10. Subscription Expiry on Colleges\n\nWhat's actually built:\n\n    collegeIsolation.middleware.js\n\n    checks\n\n    college.subscriptionExpiry\n\n    — if past expiry, blocks all requests with\n\n    SUBSCRIPTION_EXPIRED\n\n    error\n\n    Warns in logs if expiry is within 7 days\n\n    The\n\n    College\n\n    model does NOT have a\n\n    subscriptionExpiry\n\n    field — it's checked in middleware but never stored\n\nMaturity: Half-built. The enforcement logic exists in middleware but the data model doesn't support it. The\n\nCollege\n\nmodel has no\n\nsubscriptionExpiry\n\n,\n\nplan\n\n, or\n\nbillingCycle\n\nfields. So currently this check never triggers because the field is always undefined.\n\nGap: This is a critical business feature (SaaS billing) that's been started but not completed. Need to add\n\nsubscriptionExpiry\n\n,\n\nplan\n\n(TRIAL/BASIC/PREMIUM),\n\ntrialEndsAt\n\nto the College model, and a Super Admin UI to manage subscriptions.\n11. Soft Delete / Cascade Deactivation\n\nWhat's actually built:\n\n    College\n\n    model has two\n\n    pre('findOneAndUpdate')\n\n    hooks — one for soft delete (isActive → false cascades to all 14 related collections), one for restore (isActive → true restores all)\n\n    Also has\n\n    pre('findOneAndDelete')\n\n    for hard delete that removes all related data\n\n    Student deactivation (DEACTIVATED status) — separate from college deactivation\n\n    Teacher deactivation (\n\n    status: INACTIVE\n\n    )\n\n    User deactivation (\n\n    isActive: false\n\n    )\n\nMaturity: The cascade logic is thorough — covers departments, courses, students, teachers, subjects, fee structures, student fees, notifications, timetables, slots, attendance sessions, records, document configs, users. This is production-grade.\n\nGap: Two\n\npre('findOneAndUpdate')\n\nhooks on the same model for opposite operations is fragile — both hooks run on every\n\nfindOneAndUpdate\n\ncall, each checking their own condition. If both\n\nisActive: true\n\nand\n\nisActive: false\n\nare somehow in the same update (edge case), both hooks fire. Should be merged into one hook with an if/else. Also, the restore hook blindly sets all students back to APPROVED — students who were REJECTED or PENDING before the college was deactivated will incorrectly become APPROVED on restore.\nSummary for SUPER_ADMIN creates invoice/bill for college            │\n│     • Plan: BASIC/PREMIUM/ENTERPRISE                        │\n│     • Billing cycle: Annual (Apr-Mar) or Academic (Jun-May) │\n│     • GST-compliant invoice (HSN, place of supply)          │\n│     • Payment terms: Net 30/45/60 days                      │\n│     • Tender/PO reference field (optional)                  │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n         │\n         ▼\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│  2. COLLEGE_ADMIN / PRINCIPAL receives notification         │\n│     • View invoice in portal                                │\n│     • Download PDF invoice (GST-compliant)                  │\n│     • See payment instructions:                             │\n│       - Bank transfer (NEFT/RTGS/IMPS)                      │\n│       - Cheque/DD in favor of \"Lemmecode Technologies\"      │\n│       - UPI ID (optional for smaller amounts)               │\n│     • Upload payment proof:                                 │\n│       - Screenshot of bank transfer                         │\n│       - Cheque/DD photo + transaction ID                    │\n│       - PO/Tender document reference                        │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n         │\n         ▼\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│  3. SUPER_ADMIN / BILLING_MANAGER verifies payment          │\n│     • Match uploaded proof with bank statement              │\n│     • Mark invoice as: PAID / PARTIAL / REJECTED           │\n│     • If rejected: add reason, notify college to re-submit  │\n│     • If approved:                                          │\n│       - Update college.subscriptionExpiry                   │\n│       - Send payment confirmation email + updated invoice   │\n│       - Log audit trail (who verified, when, IP)            │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n         │\n         ▼\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│  4. College access continues / renews                       │\n│     • If payment not received by due date + grace period:   │\n│       - Warn at 7 days before expiry                        │\n│       - Soft-block non-critical features at expiry          │\n│       - Hard-block (read-only) after 15-day grace           │\n│       - Full suspension after 30 days (configurable)        │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n---\n\n### 🗃️ Database Schema Additions\n\n```javascript\n// backend/src/models/college.model.js (additions)\n{\n  // Billing & Subscription\n  subscription: {\n    plan: { type: String, enum: ['TRIAL', 'BASIC', 'PREMIUM', 'ENTERPRISE'], default: 'TRIAL' },\n    billingCycle: { type: String, enum: ['ANNUAL_APR_MAR', 'ACADEMIC_JUN_MAY'], default: 'ACADEMIC_JUN_MAY' },\n    subscriptionExpiry: Date, // When access ends if not renewed\n    gracePeriodDays: { type: Number, default: 15 }, // Days after expiry before hard block\n    autoRenew: { type: Boolean, default: false }, // Always false for India MVP\n  },\n\n  // Billing contact (separate from admin)\n  billingContact: {\n    name: String,\n    email: String, // Receives invoices\n    phone: String,\n    designation: String, // e.g., \"Finance Officer\", \"Bursar\"\n  },\n\n  // GST & Legal\n  gstDetails: {\n    gstin: String, // 15-digit GSTIN\n    legalName: String, // As per GST registration\n    address: String, // For invoice place-of-supply\n    stateCode: String, // 2-digit state code for GST\n  }\n}\n```\n\n```javascript\n// backend/src/models/invoice.model.js (NEW)\nconst invoiceSchema = new mongoose.Schema({\n  college_id: { type: mongoose.Schema.Types.ObjectId, ref: 'College', required: true, index: true },\n  invoiceNumber: { type: String, required: true, unique: true }, // Format: INV-2026-000123\n  invoiceDate: { type: Date, default: Date.now },\n  dueDate: { type: Date, required: true }, // Net 30/45/60 from invoiceDate\n  billingPeriod: {\n    from: Date,\n    to: Date\n  },\n  plan: { type: String, enum: ['BASIC', 'PREMIUM', 'ENTERPRISE'], required: true },\n  amount: {\n    subtotal: Number,\n    cgst: Number, // 9% for intra-state\n    sgst: Number, // 9% for intra-state\n    igst: Number, // 18% for inter-state\n    total: Number, // subtotal + tax\n    currency: { type: String, default: 'INR' }\n  },\n  gstDetails: {\n    hsnCode: String, // e.g., \"998314\" for software services\n    placeOfSupply: String, // State code\n    reverseCharge: { type: Boolean, default: false }\n  },\n  tenderReference: {\n    tenderNumber: String, // Optional: college's tender/PO number\n    poNumber: String,\n    issuedBy: String, // e.g., \"University of Mumbai\"\n    attachmentUrl: String // Upload PO/Tender PDF\n  },\n  status: {\n    type: String,\n    enum: ['DRAFT', 'SENT', 'PARTIAL', 'PAID', 'OVERDUE', 'CANCELLED'],\n    default: 'DRAFT'\n  },\n  paymentProof: {\n    uploadedBy: { type: mongoose.Schema.Types.ObjectId, ref: 'User' },\n    uploadedAt: Date,\n    files: [{\n      url: String,\n      filename: String,\n      fileType: String, // 'bank_transfer' | 'cheque' | 'dd' | 'upi'\n      referenceNumber: String, // UTR / Cheque No / DD No\n      remarks: String\n    }],\n    verifiedBy: { type: mongoose.Schema.Types.ObjectId, ref: 'User' },\n    verifiedAt: Date,\n    verificationRemarks: String\n  },\n  remindersSent: [{\n    sentAt: Date,\n    type: { type: String, enum: ['DUE_SOON', 'OVERDUE_7', 'OVERDUE_15', 'FINAL_NOTICE'] },\n    channel: { type: String, enum: ['EMAIL', 'IN_APP'] }\n  }],\n  auditLog: [{\n    action: String, // 'created', 'sent', 'proof_uploaded', 'verified', 'rejected'\n    by: { type: mongoose.Schema.Types.ObjectId, ref: 'User' },\n    at: Date,\n    ip: String,\n    notes: String\n  }],\n  createdAt: { type: Date, default: Date.now },\n  updatedAt: { type: Date, default: Date.now }\n});\n\n// Indexes\ninvoiceSchema.index({ college_id: 1, status: 1 });\ninvoiceSchema.index({ dueDate: 1, status: 1 }); // For cron job: find overdue invoices\n```\n\n---\n\n### 🔐 Role-Based Access for Billing\n\n| Role | Can View Invoices | |\n| **PRINCIPAL** | ✅ Own college only | ✅ Yes (if billingContact not set) | ❌ | ❌ |\n| **ACCOUNTANT** *(college-level)* | ✅ Own college only | ✅ Yes | ❌ | ❌ |\n\n> 💡 **Note**: `BILLING_MANAGER` is a is created & sent\n{\n  to: [college.adminEmail, college.billingContact?.email].filter(Boolean),\n  subject: `Invoice ${invoice.invoiceNumber} - ${college.name} - NOVAA Subscription`,\n  template: }\n}\n\n// When payment proof is uploaded\n{\n  to: ['billing@lemmecode.in'], // Platform finance team\n  cc: [college.adminEmail],\n  subject: `Payment Proof Uploaded - Invoice ${invoice.invoiceNumber} - ${college.name}`,\n  template: 'payment_proof_uploaded',\n  context: {\n    collegeName: college.name,\n    invoiceNumber: invoice.invoiceNumber,\n    proofFiles: invoice.paymentProof.files,\n    uploadedBy: user.name,\n    uploadedAt: formatDate(invoice.paymentProof.uploadedAt)\n  }\n}\n\n// When payment is verified & subscription renewed\n{\n  to: [college.adminEmail, college.billingContact?.email].filter(Boolean),\n  subject: `Payment Confirmed - Subscription Renewed - ${college.name}`,\n  template: 'payment_confirmed',\n  context: {\n    collegeName: college.name,\n    invoiceNumber: invoice.invoiceNumber,\n    newExpiryDate: formatDate(college.subscription.subscriptionExpiry, 'DD MMM YYYY'),\n    receiptUrl: `/api/invoices/${invoice._id}/receipt.pdf` // GST-compliant receipt\n  }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### 🔄 Cron Jobs for Billing\n\n```javascript\n// backend/src/cron/billing.cron.js\n\n// Daily: Check for overdue invoices & send reminders\ncron.schedule('0 9 * * *', async () => {\n  const today = new Date();\n  \n  // 7 days before due: gentle reminder\n  const dueSoon = await Invoice.find({\n    status: 'SENT',\n    dueDate: { $gte: today, $lte: addDays(today, 7) }\n  }).populate('college_id');\n  \n  for (const inv of dueSoon) {\n    await sendReminder(inv, 'DUE_SOON');\n  }\n  \n  // Overdue 7 days: firm reminder\n  const overdue7 = await Invoice.find({\n    status: 'SENT',\n    dueDate: { $lt: subDays(today, 7), $gte: subDays(today, 14) }\n  }).populate('college_id');\n  \n  for (const inv of overdue7) {\n    await sendReminder(inv, 'OVERDUE_7');\n    inv.status = 'OVERDUE';\n    await inv.save();\n  }\n  \n  // Overdue 15 days: final notice + soft block warning\n  const overdue15 = await Invoice.find({\n    status: 'OVERDUE',\n    dueDate: { $lt: subDays(today, 15) }\n  }).populate('college_id');\n  \n  for (const inv of overdue15) {\n    const college = inv.college_id;\n    if (college.subscriptionExpiry && new Date() > college.subscriptionExpiry) {\n      await sendFinalNotice(inv);\n      // Soft block: disable non-critical features\n      await applySoftBlock(college._id);\n    }\n  }\n});\n\n// Weekly: Generate GST-compliant monthly statements for SUPER_ADMIN\ncron.schedule('0 10 * * 1', async () => {\n  // Generate GSTR-1 style summary for platform revenue\n  // Export to CSV/PDF for CA filing\n});\n```\n\n---\n\n### 🛡️ DPDPA 2026 Compliance for Billing Data\n\n| Data Type | Retention Rule | Anonymization Rule |\n|-----------|---------------|-------------------|\n| Invoice PDFs | 8 years (GST law) | N/A — legal requirement |\n| Payment proofs (bank screenshots) | 3 years post-contract end | Blur account numbers after 1 year |\n| GSTIN, legal name | Permanent (as long as college exists) | N/A |\n| Billing contact personal data | Delete 1 year after contract end | Anonymize name/email, keep role |\n| Audit logs (who verified payment) | 5 years | Keep action/timestamp, anonymize user ID after 2 years |\n\n> ✅ Implement `rightToErasure` workflow: College can request deletion of non-essential billing data; system flags GST-mandated data as \"legal hold\".\n\n---\n\n## 🎯 Immediate Next Steps (This Week)\n\n1. ✅ **Add `subscription` and `gstDetails` fields to College model** (migration script)\n2. ✅ 📋 Boss Feedback Analysis — NOVAA/Smart College\n\n> ✅ No code included — pure business logic, workflow clarification, and product recommendations.\n\n---\n\n## 🔐 Question 1: Login Credential Delivery\n\n### Boss's Concern\n> *\"If Gmail is not allowed due to config issues, can sales person provide credentials manually at onboarding?\"*\n\n### What This Means\n| Current Assumption | Boss's Reality |\n|-------------------|----------------|\n| System auto-emails credentials to college admin | Email delivery may fail (SPF/DKIM, college IT policies) |\n| College admin receives credentials digitally | Sales rep is physically present during onboarding — can hand over credentials in person |\n| Password change is optional | Admin should be **prompted to change password immediately** on first login |\n\n### Recommended Workflow\n```\n1. SUPER_ADMIN / LemmeCode team creates college tenant + admin user\n2. System generates temporary credentials (username + random password)\n3. Credentials displayed ONLY to:\n   - LemmeCode onboarding team (internal dashboard)\n   - Assigned Sales Representative (via secure internal portal)\n4. Sales rep shares credentials with College Admin:\n   - In-person during demo/onboarding session, OR\n   - Via encrypted WhatsApp/Signal, OR\n   - Printed handover sheet (collected after first login)\n5. On first login, system forces password reset + MFA setup (optional)\n6. Temporary credentials expire after 24 hours or first use\n```\n\n### Action Items\n- ✅ Add \"Credential Handover\" view in SUPER_ADMIN dashboard (visible only to internal roles)\n- ✅ Add mandatory \"Change Password on First Login\" prompt\n- ✅ Add credential expiry logic (24-hour TTL for temp passwords)\n- ❌ Do NOT give sales reps backend access or data entry permissions\n\n---\n\n## 🎓 Role 2: College Admin → Course Management Enhancement\n\n### Boss's Request\n> *\"Add fields: Course Name, Number of Semesters, Class/Year (FY | SY | TY | Final Year)\"*\n\n### Why This Matters (Indian Context)\n| Global Terminology | Indian Student Reality |\n|-------------------|------------------------|\n| \"Semester 5\" | \"TY B.Sc Computer Science\" (Third Year) |\n| \"Year 2, Term 1\" | \"SY B.Com Division A\" |\n| \"Progress by credit\" | \"Promoted if passed ≥ X subjects\" |\n\nStudents, parents, and college staff think in **Academic Years**, not just semesters. Promotion, timetables, and reporting must align with this mental model.\n\n### Recommended Data Model Adjustment\n```\nCourse Entity:\n- courseName: \"Bachelor of Computer Science\"\n- shortName: \"BCS\"\n- totalSemesters: 6\n- academicYearMapping: [\n    { yearLabel: \"FY\", semesters: [1, 2] },\n    { yearLabel: \"SY\", semesters: [3, 4] },\n    { yearLabel: \"TY\", semesters: [5, 6] }\n  ]\n- promotionRule: \"PASS_MIN_SUBJECTS\" | \"NO_ATKT\" | \"CUSTOM\"\n```\n\n### Action Items\n- ✅ Add `academicYearLabel` (FY/SY/TY/Final) to Course and Student enrollment records\n- ✅ Update promotion logic to evaluate by **Year + Subject Pass Count**, not just fee status\n- ✅ Display \"TY BCS\" in UI everywhere instead of \"Semester 5\" for Indian colleges\n- ✅ Allow colleges to customize year labels (some use \"First Year\", others \"FY\")\n\n---\n\n## 👨‍🏫 Role 2: College Admin → Teacher Management + Classroom Assignment\n\n### Boss's Request\n> *\"Assign teacher to classrooms/divisions. Example: Mrs. Shradhha Kapoor teaches PHP to FY (Room 105) and SY (Room 201).\"*\n\n### What This Solves\n| Problem | Solution |\n|---------|----------|\n| Timetable conflicts (two classes booked in same room) | Room-level booking validation |\n| Confusion: \"Which class is where?\" | Clear room + division mapping in timetable |\n| HOD/Admin spends time resolving scheduling conflicts | System prevents double-booking at entry |\n\n### Recommended Workflow\n```\nTeacher Assignment Form:\n1. Select Teacher → Mrs. Shradhha Kapoor\n2. Select Subject → PHP\n3. Assign to Academic Years:\n   ☑ FY (First Year) → Room: 105, Division: A, Time Slot: 10am-11am\n   ☑ SY (Second Year) → Room: 201, Division: B, Time Slot: 1pm-2pm\n4. System validates:\n   - Room 105 not already booked for FY at 10am-11am\n   - Teacher not double-booked at same time\n5. Timetable auto-generates with room + division labels\n```\n\n### Action Items\n- ✅ Add `roomNumber` and `division` fields to timetable slot creation\n- ✅ Add room-availability validation during timetable creation\n- ✅ Display room + division in teacher/student timetable views\n- ✅ Allow HOD to manage room assignments for their department only\n\n---\n\n## 🎓 Role 2: Student Admission Workflow Clarification\n\n### Boss's Concern\n> *\"Approval ≠ Enrollment. Student may get approved by multiple colleges but choose only one. Credentials should be sent only after confirmed admission + fee payment.\"*\n\n### Current Gap vs. Reality\n| System Assumes | Indian Reality |\n|---------------|----------------|\n| Approve student → send login → student is enrolled | Student applies to 5-10 colleges → gets 3 approvals → chooses 1 → pays admission fee → then becomes active |\n| Credentials sent at approval | Credentials sent only after **confirmed admission + down payment** |\n| One application = one enrollment | Multiple parallel applications; only one converts |\n\n### Recommended Workflow\n```\nStudent Application Flow:\n1. Student submits application → Status: \"SUBMITTED\"\n2. Admin reviews → Status: \"APPROVED\" (conditional)\n3. College contacts student (call/email) → \"You're approved! Confirm admission?\"\n4. Student visits college, pays admission fee/down payment\n5. Admin marks: \"ADMISSION_CONFIRMED\" + \"FEE_PARTIAL_PAID\"\n6. SYSTEM TRIGGERS: \n   - Generate student login credentials\n   - Send welcome email/SMS with login instructions\n   - Activate student dashboard access\n7. Student logs in, completes profile, views timetable/fees\n```\n\n### Action Items\n- ✅ Add admission status enum: `SUBMITTED` → `APPROVED` → `CONFIRMED` → `ENROLLED`\n- ✅ Decouple credential generation from \"APPROVED\" status → trigger only on `CONFIRMED + FEE_PAID`\n- ✅ Add \"Send Credentials\" manual trigger for Admin (with audit log)\n- ✅ Add reminder workflow: \"Approved but not confirmed in 7 days\" → notify admin\n\n---\n\n## 📈 Role 2: Student Promotion Logic — Results Over Fees\n\n### Boss's Clarification\n> *\"Promotion depends on exam results (subjects passed, ATKT count), not just fee payment. Students can get re-evaluation or October re-attempt. Advance booking for next year is possible.\"*\n\n### Critical Business Rule\n```\nPromotion Eligibility = \n  (Fee Status: FULLY_PAID OR PARTIALLY_PAID_WITH_APPROVAL) \n  AND \n  (Academic Status: PASS_THRESHOLD_MET OR REATTEMPT_PENDING)\n```\n\n### Indian Academic Nuances to Support\n| Scenario | System Handling |\n|----------|----------------|\n| Student paid full fee but failed 4/6 subjects | ❌ Block promotion; show \"ATKT: 4 subjects pending\" |\n| Student paid partial fee but passed all subjects | ⚠️ Allow promotion with admin override + remark |\n| Student failed, applied for re-evaluation | ⚠️ Allow \"provisional promotion\" with flag; auto-review when results updated |\n| Student booked next year in advance (confident of passing re-attempt) | ✅ Allow \"advance enrollment\" with conditional status |\n| October re-attempt results arrive later | ✅ Auto-update promotion status; notify student/admin |\n\n### Action Items\n- ✅ Add `academicResult` model: subject-wise marks, pass/fail, ATKT count, reattempt status\n- ✅ Update promotion logic to evaluate: `passedSubjects >= requiredThreshold`\n- ✅ Add \"Provisional Promotion\" status for re-evaluation/reattempt cases\n- ✅ Add admin override option with mandatory remark + expiry date\n- ✅ Auto-trigger promotion re-evaluation when re-attempt results are entered\n\n---\n\n## 👨‍💼 Role 3: HOD as Teacher — Timetable Exception\n\n### Boss's Clarification\n> *\"HOD is also a teacher. They create timetables for their department's teachers, AND manage their own teaching schedule. No one else creates HOD's timetable.\"*\n\n### Current Design Gap\n| Assumption | Reality |\n|-----------|---------|\n| HOD is a permission overlay on Teacher | ✅ Correct |\n| HOD can manage timetables for dept teachers | ✅ Correct |\n| But who creates HOD's own teaching slots? | ❌ Not addressed — HOD must self-manage |\n\n### Recommended Workflow\n```\nHOD Timetable Access:\n1. HOD logs in → sees TWO views:\n   A. \"My Teaching Schedule\" (read-only for others, editable by HOD)\n   B. \"Department Timetable\" (manage all teachers in Electronics dept)\n2. When creating slot for self:\n   - System auto-fills: Teacher = Current User (HOD)\n   - Room selection respects department room pool\n3. When creating slot for other teacher:\n   - Dropdown shows only teachers in same department\n   - Room selection respects department room pool\n4. Conflict validation applies to ALL slots (including HOD's own)\n```\n\n### Action Items\n- ✅ Ensure HOD can edit their own teaching slots (not just others')\n- ✅ Filter teacher dropdown in timetable builder by department\n- ✅ Filter room dropdown by department-assigned rooms\n- ✅ Add visual indicator: \"Your Slot\" vs \"Managed Slot\" in HOD timetable view\n\n---\n\n## 👨‍🎓 Role 4: Student → Category Certificate Logic\n\n### Boss's Note\n> *\"Category certificate upload is automatically skipped for General category students. Mandatory for all others.\"*\n\n### Clarification Needed\nThe current logic is correct, but the documentation must be explicit:\n\n```\nDocument Requirement Logic:\nIF student.category == \"GENERAL\" \n  → Skip \"Category Certificate\" field entirely (do not show)\nELSE \n  → Mark \"Category Certificate\" as MANDATORY\n  → Allowed formats: PDF, JPG, PNG\n  → Max size: 5MB\n  → Description: \"Valid caste/category certificate issued by competent authority\"\n```\n\n### Action Items\n- ✅ Update `DocumentConfig` logic to conditionally hide (not just disable) category certificate for GENERAL\n- ✅ Add tooltip/explainer: \"General category students are not required to submit this document\"\n- ✅ Ensure backend validation mirrors frontend logic (no bypass via API)\n\n---\n\n## 🆕 New Module Requests (High-Level Scope)\n\nBoss requested several new capabilities. Here's how to categorize them:\n\n### 📊 Expense & Accounts Module (V1.1 Priority)\n| Component | Purpose | Indian Context |\n|-----------|---------|---------------|\n| **Vendor Management** | Track housekeeping, security, gardeners, utilities | Many colleges outsource these; need vendor-wise expense tracking |\n| **Expense Categories** | Electricity, internet, renovation, marketing, extracurricular | GST-compliant categorization for audit |\n| **Biometric Attendance Integration** | Import Excel from biometric devices → calculate payroll | Most Indian colleges use Excel exports from devices like eSSL, Hikvision |\n| **Payroll Engine** | Calculate salary based on attendance, leaves, deductions | PF, ESI, professional tax, TDS compliance |\n| **Income Tracking** | Admission fees, exam fees, donation, grants | Map income to budget heads for NAAC/NIRF reporting |\n\n### 🪪 Student Services Module (V1.0 Low-Effort Wins)\n| Feature | Purpose | Priority |\n|---------|---------|----------|\n| **ID Card Generator** | Bulk print student ID cards with photo, course, year, barcode | 🔴 High (needed at admission start) |\n| **Hall Ticket Generator** | Exam hall tickets with photo, seat no., timetable, rules | 🔴 High (pre-exam rush) |\n| **Result Transcript** | Year-wise results: passed/failed, marks, percentage, ATKT status | 🟡 Medium |\n| **Re-evaluation Request** | Student applies for re-checking; admin forwards to university | 🟡 Medium |\n| **Degree/Provisional Certificate** | Auto-generate draft degree on completion; print-ready | 🟢 Low (end-of-cycle) |\n\n### 📅 Academic Enhancement (V1.1)\n| Feature | Purpose |\n|---------|---------|\n| **Faculty Leave Management** | Apply/approve leaves; auto-adjust timetable; sync with payroll |\n| **MCQ Test Engine** | Topic-wise/monthly tests; auto-evaluate; generate performance reports |\n| **Marketing Expense Tracker** | Track campaign spend vs. admission conversions |\n\n---\n\n## 🎯 Prioritized Action Summary\n\n### 🔴 Immediate (V1.0 Launch Blockers)\n1. Fix login credential delivery workflow (manual handover + forced password reset)\n2. Add academic year labels (FY/SY/TY) to Course + Student models\n3. Add room + division assignment to Teacher + Timetable modules\n4. Decouple student credentials from \"approved\" status → trigger on \"confirmed + fee paid\"\n5. Update promotion logic to evaluate academic results, not just fees\n6. Clarify category certificate logic in docs + enforce backend validation\n\n### 🟡 Short-Term (V1.0 Nice-to-Have)\n7. Add \"provisional promotion\" status for re-evaluation cases\n8. Ensure HOD can manage their own teaching slots\n9. Build ID card + hall ticket PDF generators (use existing student data)\n10. Add expense category scaffolding (even if payroll comes later)\n\n### 🟢 Medium-Term (V1.1 Planning)\n11. Design Expense & Payroll module schema (vendor, attendance import, salary calc)\n12. Build biometric Excel import utility (CSV mapping config)\n13. Add re-evaluation workflow + university forwarding template\n14. Implement faculty leave management + timetable auto-adjust\n\n---\n\n## 💡 Strategic Recommendations\n\n1. **Document Indian terminology upfront**  \n   Create a glossary: FY/SY/TY, ATKT, Provisional Admission, Category Certificate, etc. — use it consistently in UI + docs.\n\n2. **Separate \"Approval\" from \"Enrollment\" in all workflows**  \n   This is the #1 source of confusion in Indian admissions. Make the status transitions explicit in UI and API.\n\n3. **Design for \"Advance Booking\" patterns**  \n   Indian students often secure next-year seats before results. Support conditional enrollment with expiry.\n\n4. **Keep payroll/expense module modular**  \n   Start with expense tracking + vendor management. Add biometric import + salary calc in V1.1 after core academic modules stabilize.\n\n5. **Leverage existing PDF generation**  \n   You already generate fee receipts. Reuse that engine for ID cards, hall tickets, and provisional certificates — minimal new code.\n\n---\n\n> ✅ **Final Note**: Your boss is thinking like a college operator — not a SaaS product manager. Every request ties back to real workflows: admission season chaos, exam timetable conflicts, fee collection pressure, NAAC audit prep.  \n>   \n> **Recommendation**: Before building anything new, validate each workflow with 2-3 pilot college admins. Their feedback will save weeks of rework.\n\nNeed me to draft the updated workflow diagrams or user stories for any of the above? 📋 Module Review & Action Plan — NOVAA/Smart College\n\n> ✅ Your analysis is excellent — thorough, honest, and production-aware. Below: prioritized actions per module + detailed subscription/billing workflow for Indian institutional context.\n\n---\n\n## 🎯 Module-by-Module Recommendations\n\n| Module | Maturity | Action | Priority | Notes |\n|--------|----------|--------|----------|-------|\n| **Timetable** | ✅ Production-grade | 📝 Document as V1.0 feature | 🔴 Critical | Wire up `notifyAffected()` on exception approval; add approval audit log |\n| **Teacher Attendance** | ⚠️ Partial (lecture report) | 🔄 Rename to \"Teacher Lecture Report\"; flag real teacher attendance as V1.2 | 🟡 Medium | Add separate `TeacherPresence` model later for NAAC/salary compliance |\n| **Student Promotion/Alumni** | ✅ Solid | 📝 Document as V1.0; add promotion email + bulk fee-override | 🟡 Medium | Email template + DPDPA consent for alumni data retention |\n| **Installment Payments** | ✅ Solid | 📝 Document as V1.0; add due-date enforcement + late-fee logic | 🔴 Critical | Late fee = configurable % or fixed; reminder cron must check per-installment |\n| **Offline Payment Recording** | ✅ Complete | 📝 Document as V1.0; add offline receipt PDF generation | 🔴 Critical | Receipt must include admin name, timestamp, reference number, college seal placeholder |\n| **Stripe Gateway** | ✅ Built but misaligned | ⚠️ Deprecate for India MVP; keep code but hide from UI; document Razorpay as primary | 🟢 Low | Revisit if expanding to NRI/international student payments later |\n| **Configurable Document Requirements** | ✅ Impressive | 📝 Document as V1.0 differentiator; add config versioning + audit trail | 🔴 Critical | Versioning prevents mid-cycle config changes breaking submitted applications |\n| **HOD Role** | ✅ Clean design | 📝 Document as V1.0; expand permissions to leave approval + dept reports | 🟡 Medium | Keep as permission overlay (not enum role) — avoids role explosion |\n| **Notification System** | ✅ Well-designed | 📝 Document as V1.0; add email trigger + actionUrl routing + expiry enforcement | 🟡 Medium | Email fallback critical for low-connectivity Indian colleges |\n| **Subscription Expiry** | ❌ Half-built | 🔧 Redesign for institutional billing (see detailed workflow below) | 🔴 Critical | Middleware exists but model missing — fix before pilot launch |\n| **Soft Delete / Cascade** | ✅ Thorough | 🐛 Fix restore hook bug; merge duplicate pre-hooks; document as V1.0 | 🔴 Critical | Restore must preserve original student statuses, not force APPROVED |\n\n---\n\n## 💰 Subscription & Billing Workflow — Indian Institutional Context\n\n> ❌ Not a typical SaaS credit-card flow  \n> ✅ Tender → Invoice → Offline Payment → Proof Upload → Verification → Activation\n\n### 🔄 End-to-End Flow\n\n```\n1. SUPER_ADMIN creates billing cycle\n   │\n   ▼\n2. System generates Invoice (PDF) with:\n   • College name, GSTIN, address\n   • Plan type (BASIC/PREMIUM/ENTERPRISE)\n   • Amount, GST breakdown, due date\n   • Payment instructions: Bank transfer / DD / Cheque details\n   • Unique Invoice ID + QR code (for reconciliation)\n   │\n   ▼\n3. Invoice sent to:\n   • COLLEGE_ADMIN (primary)\n   • PRINCIPAL / REGISTRAR (secondary approver)\n   • Optional: Finance email from college master data\n   │\n   ▼\n4. College makes offline payment:\n   • Bank transfer / DD / Cheque / Cash at counter\n   • Gets transaction reference / UTR / DD number\n   │\n   ▼\n5. COLLEGE_ADMIN or PRINCIPAL logs in → \"Billing\" section:\n   • Selects outstanding invoice\n   • Uploads payment proof: scanned cheque/DD, bank screenshot, UTR\n   • Adds remarks: \"Paid via DD No. XXX, Bank: SBI, Date: DD/MM/YYYY\"\n   • Submits for verification\n   │\n   ▼\n6. SUPER_ADMIN (or PLATFORM_SUPPORT) receives notification:\n   • Reviews payment proof\n   • Matches UTR/DD number with bank statement\n   • Approves → subscriptionExpiry extended + activation confirmed\n   • OR Rejects → requests clarification with comment\n   │\n   ▼\n7. System actions on approval:\n   • Updates college.subscriptionExpiry\n   • Sends confirmation email to college contacts\n   • Generates official receipt PDF (with digital signature placeholder)\n   • Logs audit entry: who approved, when, proof reference\n   │\n   ▼\n8. If payment not received by due date:\n   • Day -7: Warning email to COLLEGE_ADMIN + PRINCIPAL\n   • Day 0: Subscription marked \"PENDING_EXPIRY\" — read-only mode\n   • Day +7: Subscription \"EXPIRED\" — access blocked (collegeIsolation middleware)\n   • Grace period: 15 days for tender-delay scenarios (configurable per college)\n```\n\n---\n\n## 👥 Role Permissions for Billing Flow\n\n| Role | Billing Permissions |\n|------|-------------------|\n| **SUPER_ADMIN** | • Create/edit invoices<br>• View all college payment proofs<br>• Approve/reject payments<br>• Extend subscription expiry<br>• Export billing reports (GST-compliant) |\n| **PLATFORM_SUPPORT** | • View invoices & proofs (read-only)<br>• Escalate disputed payments<br>• Cannot approve/reject |\n| **COLLEGE_ADMIN** | • View college invoices<br>• Upload payment proof<br>• View payment status<br>• Download receipts<br>• Request invoice correction |\n| **PRINCIPAL** | • View invoices (read-only)<br>• Upload payment proof *(secondary payer)*<br>• Receive payment confirmations<br>• Cannot edit invoice details |\n| **ACCOUNTANT** *(college-level)* | • View fee-related invoices only<br>• Upload payment proof for fee-module subscriptions<br>• Cannot access platform subscription billing |\n\n> 🔐 **Audit Requirement**: Every billing action (invoice creation, proof upload, approval) must log: `actor_id`, `timestamp`, `ip_address`, `action_type`, `invoice_id`, `proof_reference`.\n\n---\n\n## 📄 Invoice & Receipt Requirements (India Compliance)\n\n### Invoice Must Include:\n- College legal name + registered address\n- GSTIN of NOVAA entity + college GSTIN (if applicable)\n- Invoice number (sequential, financial-year prefixed: `INV/2026-27/00123`)\n- Date of issue + due date (Net 30 typical for institutions)\n- Line items: Plan name, base amount, CGST/SGST/IGST breakdown\n- Payment instructions: Bank name, account number, IFSC, UPI ID (for reference)\n- Unique QR code (for fast reconciliation)\n- Digital signature placeholder (for future e-sign integration)\n\n### Receipt Must Include:\n- \"OFFICIAL RECEIPT\" header\n- Reference to original invoice ID\n- Payment mode: Bank Transfer / DD / Cheque / Cash\n- Transaction reference: UTR / DD Number / Cheque Number\n- Amount received + date of credit\n- Authorized signatory name + designation (SUPER_ADMIN or delegated)\n- DPDPA note: \"This receipt confirms payment; personal data processed per consent\"\n\n---\n\n## 🗂️ Data Model Additions (Conceptual — No Code)\n\n### College Model Extensions:\n- `subscriptionPlan`: enum [TRIAL, BASIC, PREMIUM, ENTERPRISE, CUSTOM]\n- `subscriptionExpiry`: Date\n- `billingContactEmail`: String (separate from admin email)\n- `billingContactPhone`: String (for payment reminders)\n- `gstNumber`: String (college GSTIN)\n- `purchaseOrderRequired`: Boolean (some colleges need PO before payment)\n- `tenderReference`: String (if payment linked to government tender)\n\n### Invoice Model (New):\n- `college_id`: ObjectId (ref: College)\n- `invoiceNumber`: String (unique, indexed)\n- `financialYear`: String (e.g., \"2026-27\")\n- `plan`: String\n- `baseAmount`, `gstAmount`, `totalAmount`: Number\n- `issueDate`, `dueDate`, `paidDate`: Date\n- `status`: enum [DRAFT, ISSUED, PAID, OVERDUE, CANCELLED, DISPUTED]\n- `paymentProof`: { uploadedBy, uploadedAt, fileUrl, referenceNumber, remarks }\n- `approvedBy`: ObjectId (ref: User)\n- `approvedAt`: Date\n- `receiptGenerated`: Boolean\n- `auditLog`: [{ action, by, at, notes }]\n\n### Notification Extensions:\n- New type: `BILLING`\n- New targeting: `BILLING_CONTACTS` (uses college.billingContactEmail)\n- ActionUrl routing: `/billing/invoices/:invoiceId`\n\n---\n\n## 🇮🇳 India-Specific Billing Considerations\n\n| Requirement | Implementation Guidance |\n|-------------|------------------------|\n| **Tender-based procurement** | Allow `tenderReference` field; support PO upload before invoice generation; flexible due dates |\n| **GST compliance** | Auto-calculate CGST/SGST (intra-state) or IGST (inter-state); generate GSTR-1 compatible export |\n| **Financial year alignment** | Invoices dated Apr 1 – Mar 31; renewal cycles can align with academic year (June–May) if needed |\n| **Multi-signatory approvals** | Support \"requires 2 approvals\" flag for government colleges; PRINCIPAL + ACCOUNTANT co-sign |\n| **Payment proof formats** | Accept PDF, JPG, PNG for scanned cheques/DD; max 5MB; virus scan on upload |\n| **DPDPA consent for billing data** | Explicit consent checkbox during college onboarding: \"We process billing data for invoicing and compliance\" |\n| **Grace periods for government delays** | Configurable `gracePeriodDays` per college; auto-extend expiry if tender approval delayed |\n\n---\n\n## 🚨 Critical Fixes Before Pilot Launch\n\n1. **Subscription Model Gap**  \n   → Add `subscriptionExpiry`, `plan`, `billingContact*` fields to College model  \n   → Build SUPER_ADMIN invoice creation UI (minimal: form + PDF preview)  \n   → Build COLLEGE_ADMIN payment proof upload UI  \n\n2. **Soft Delete Restore Bug**  \n   → Merge duplicate `pre('findOneAndUpdate')` hooks  \n   → Fix restore logic: preserve original student/teacher statuses, don't force APPROVED  \n\n3. **Offline Payment Receipts**  \n   → Generate PDF receipt on proof approval (mirror online payment receipt Fix College model + build minimal invoice CRUD for SUPER_ADMIN\n2. Build payment proof upload + approval flow (COLLEGE_ADMIN → SUPER_ADMIN)\n3. Timetable Module\n\nWhat's actually built:\n\n    Timetable\n\n    — one per department/course/semester/academic year, has DRAFT → PUBLISHED → ARCHIVED lifecycle, date range with working days, IST timezone\n\n    TimetableSlot\n\n    — individual class slots (day, startTime, endTime, subject, teacher, room, LECTURE/LAB type)\n\n    TimetableException\n\n    — 8 exception types: HOLIDAY, CANCELLED, EXTRA, RESCHEDULED, ROOM_CHANGE, TEACHER_CHANGE, SPECIAL_EVENT, EXAM. Has full approval workflow (PENDING → APPROVED/REJECTED), recurring patterns, substitute teacher support\n\n    HOD middleware — only the HOD of a department can create/manage timetables for that department\n\n    Student timetable view, teacher schedule view, weekly timetable UI\n\nMaturity: This is a fully thought-out, production-grade module. The exception model alone is more sophisticated than most commercial college systems. The slot snapshot in attendance sessions (preserving timetable state at time of session) is a smart design decision.\n\nGap: Exception notifications are modelled (\n\nnotifyAffected\n\n,\n\nnotificationsSent\n\nfields) but the actual notification sending when an exception is approved is not wired up.\n2. Teacher Attendance\n\nWhat's actually built:\n\n    teacherAttendance.controller.js\n\n    — generates a report of all closed sessions a teacher conducted, with present/absent counts and percentage per lecture\n\n    This is a teacher's own teaching record, not a separate attendance system for tracking whether teachers showed up\n\nWhat it is NOT:\n\n    There is no system to track whether a teacher was present or absent on a given day\n\n    No admin view of teacher attendance\n\n    No teacher attendance marking by admin or principal\n\nMaturity: Partial. What exists is a teacher's lecture delivery report, not teacher attendance management. The naming is misleading — it should be called \"Teacher Lecture Report.\"\n\nGap: If colleges need to track teacher presence (which they do for salary, NAAC), this needs a separate model and workflow.\n3. Student Promotion / Alumni\n\nWhat's actually built:\n\n    PromotionHistory\n\n    model — tracks fromSemester → toSemester, fromAcademicYear → toAcademicYear, fee status at time of promotion, who promoted, remarks, reversible\n\n    promoteStudent\n\n    and\n\n    bulkPromoteStudents\n\n    — admin can promote individual or bulk students\n\n    getPromotionEligibleStudents\n\n    — filters APPROVED students, shows fee status\n\n    isFinalSemesterPromotion\n\n    flag — when student completes final semester, status moves to ALUMNI\n\n    Student model has\n\n    currentSemester\n\n    ,\n\n    currentYear\n\n    (auto-calculated),\n\n    currentAcademicYear\n\n    ,\n\n    isPromotionEligible\n\n    ,\n\n    promotionHistory[]\n\nMaturity: Solid. The fee status check at promotion time (FULLY_PAID / PARTIALLY_PAID / PENDING) is a real business requirement — colleges won't promote students with pending fees. The reversal capability is also well thought out.\n\nGap: No email/notification sent to student when promoted. No bulk promotion with fee override (e.g., promote despite pending fees with admin justification).\n4. Installment-Based Payments\n\nWhat's actually built:\n\n    FeeStructure\n\n    — defined per college + course + category (GEN/OBC/SC/ST/EWS), has\n\n    installments[]\n\n    array with name, amount, dueDate\n\n    StudentFee\n\n    — per student, mirrors the fee structure installments, tracks status (PENDING/PAID/FAILED/CANCELLED) per installment, paidAmount vs totalFee\n\n    Atomic update on payment — uses\n\n    updateOne\n\n    with\n\n    status: \"PENDING\"\n\n    condition to prevent race conditions\n\n    Duplicate payment protection at two layers (status check + paymentId check)\n\nMaturity: Very solid. The category-based fee structure (different fees for SC/ST vs GEN) is a real Indian college requirement. The atomic update pattern is correct.\n\nGap: No due date enforcement — a student can pay installment 2 before installment 1. No late payment penalty logic. No installment due date reminder (the cron exists but needs to be verified it checks per-installment due dates).\n5. Offline Payment Recording\n\nWhat's actually built:\n\n    StudentFee.installments\n\n    has\n\n    paymentMode\n\n    (ONLINE/CASH/CHEQUE/DD),\n\n    referenceNumber\n\n    (for cheque/DD),\n\n    remarks\n\n    ,\n\n    markedByAdmin\n\n    Admin can mark an installment as paid offline with mode, reference number, and remarks\n\n    Full audit trail — which admin marked it, when\n\nMaturity: Complete and well-designed. This is critical for Indian colleges where many students still pay by cash or DD at the counter.\n\nGap: No receipt generation for offline payments. Online payments generate a PDF receipt via email — offline payments should too.\n6. Stripe Gateway\n\nWhat's actually built:\n\n    Full Stripe integration parallel to Razorpay\n\n    CollegePaymentConfig\n\n    — each college configures their own gateway (stripe or razorpay), credentials stored encrypted using AES-256-GCM\n\n    Per-college gateway instances cached in memory (5min TTL)\n\n    Stripe webhook handler\n\n    College admin UI to configure Stripe keys\n\nMaturity: The architecture is good — per-college payment credentials with encryption is the right approach. The encryption uses PBKDF2 key derivation which is solid.\n\nGap: Having both Stripe and Razorpay creates confusion. Razorpay is the right choice for India (UPI, Indian cards, net banking). Stripe is primarily for international cards. For MVP targeting Maharashtra colleges, Stripe adds complexity with no benefit. Decision needed: keep both but document when to use which, or deprecate Stripe for V1.\n7. Configurable Document Requirements\n\nWhat's actually built:\n\n    DocumentConfig\n\n    — per college, per\n\n    collegeCode\n\n    , list of document types each with: enabled/disabled toggle, mandatory flag, allowed formats, max file size (1-20MB), description, display order\n\n    18 document types supported: 10th marksheet, 12th marksheet, passport photo, category certificate, income certificate, character certificate, transfer certificate, Aadhaar, entrance exam score, migration certificate, domicile certificate, caste certificate, non-creamy layer, physically challenged, sports quota, NRI sponsor, gap certificate, affidavit\n\n    Student registration dynamically validates against the college's config\n\n    Category certificate skipped automatically if student is GEN category\n\nMaturity: This is genuinely impressive. Most college systems hardcode document requirements. This is fully configurable per college, which is exactly what's needed for Maharashtra's varied institution types (arts, science, engineering, medical all have different requirements).\n\nGap: No UI for admin to configure document requirements (the\n\nDocumentSettings.jsx\n\npage exists in frontend but needs verification it's fully wired). No version history — if a college changes document config mid-admission season, students who already submitted may be affected.\n8. HOD Role\n\nWhat's actually built:\n\n    HOD is a teacher with elevated timetable permissions, not a separate role in the ROLE enum\n\n    Department\n\n    model has\n\n    hod_id\n\n    field pointing to a Teacher\n\n    hod.middleware.js\n\n    — checks if the requesting teacher is the HOD of the department that owns the timetable\n\n    HOD can create, edit, publish timetables and manage slots for their department only\n\n    AssignHod.jsx\n\n    — admin UI to assign a teacher as HOD\n\nMaturity: Clean design — HOD is a permission layer on top of TEACHER, not a separate role. This avoids role explosion.\n\nGap: HOD has no other elevated permissions beyond timetable management. In reality, HODs also approve leave, manage department reports, approve timetable exceptions. The exception approval workflow exists in the model but it's not clear if HOD is the approver or admin.\n9. Notification System\n\nWhat's actually built:\n\n    Notification\n\n    model — college-scoped, created by COLLEGE_ADMIN or TEACHER\n\n    8 notification types: GENERAL, ACADEMIC, EXAM, FEE, ATTENDANCE, EVENT, ASSIGNMENT, URGENT\n\n    7 targeting options: ALL, STUDENTS, TEACHERS, DEPARTMENT, COURSE, SEMESTER, INDIVIDUAL\n\n    NotificationRead\n\n    — separate model tracking read status per user (not a field on notification itself — correct design for broadcast notifications)\n\n    Unread count API per role\n\n    Admin and teacher can create, update, delete notifications\n\nMaturity: Well-designed. The separate read-tracking model is the right approach for broadcast notifications (avoids storing one record per user per notification). Granular targeting (by department, course, semester) is a real need.\n\nGap: Notifications are in-app only — no push notifications, no email trigger from notification creation. The\n\nactionUrl\n\nfield exists but no frontend routing based on it. No notification expiry enforcement (the\n\nexpiresAt\n\nfield exists but nothing checks it).\n10. Subscription Expiry on Colleges\n\nWhat's actually built:\n\n    collegeIsolation.middleware.js\n\n    checks\n\n    college.subscriptionExpiry\n\n    — if past expiry, blocks all requests with\n\n    SUBSCRIPTION_EXPIRED\n\n    error\n\n    Warns in logs if expiry is within 7 days\n\n    The\n\n    College\n\n    model does NOT have a\n\n    subscriptionExpiry\n\n    field — it's checked in middleware but never stored\n\nMaturity: Half-built. The enforcement logic exists in middleware but the data model doesn't support it. The\n\nCollege\n\nmodel has no\n\nsubscriptionExpiry\n\n,\n\nplan\n\n, or\n\nbillingCycle\n\nfields. So currently this check never triggers because the field is always undefined.\n\nGap: This is a critical business feature (SaaS billing) that's been started but not completed. Need to add\n\nsubscriptionExpiry\n\n,\n\nplan\n\n(TRIAL/BASIC/PREMIUM),\n\ntrialEndsAt\n\nto the College model, and a Super Admin UI to manage subscriptions.\n11. Soft Delete / Cascade Deactivation\n\nWhat's actually built:\n\n    College\n\n    model has two\n\n    pre('findOneAndUpdate')\n\n    hooks — one for soft delete (isActive → false cascades to all 14 related collections), one for restore (isActive → true restores all)\n\n    Also has\n\n    pre('findOneAndDelete')\n\n    for hard delete that removes all related data\n\n    Student deactivation (DEACTIVATED status) — separate from college deactivation\n\n    Teacher deactivation (\n\n    status: INACTIVE\n\n    )\n\n    User deactivation (\n\n    isActive: false\n\n    )\n\nMaturity: The cascade logic is thorough — covers departments, courses, students, teachers, subjects, fee structures, student fees, notifications, timetables, slots, attendance sessions, records, document configs, users. This is production-grade.\n\nGap: Two\n\npre('findOneAndUpdate')\n\nhooks on the same model for opposite operations is fragile — both hooks run on every\n\nfindOneAndUpdate\n\ncall, each checking their own condition. If both\n\nisActive: true\n\nand\n\nisActive: false\n\nare somehow in the same update (edge case), both hooks fire. Should be merged into one hook with an if/else. Also, the restore hook blindly sets all students back to APPROVED — students who were REJECTED or PENDING before the college was deactivated will incorrectly become APPROVED on restore.\nSummary for
