📋 NOVAA/Smart College — Module Specifications for PRD\n\n> **Document Purpose**: Product Requirements Document (PRD) appendix — technical module specifications for development, QA, and stakeholder alignment  \n> **Target Audience**: Product Managers, Engineering Leads, QA, Compliance, Client Success  \n> **Version**: 1.0 | **Date**: April 14, 2026\n\n---\n\n## 1️⃣ Timetable Management Module\n\n### Description\nA production-grade scheduling system for academic timetables with support for department/course/semester scoping, slot-level granularity, and exception handling with approval workflows.\n\n### Key Features\n- Timetable entity with lifecycle: `DRAFT` → `PUBLISHED` → `ARCHIVED`\n- Slot-level definition: day, time range, subject, teacher, room, type (LECTURE/LAB)\n- 8 exception types: HOLIDAY, CANCELLED, EXTRA, RESCHEDULED, ROOM_CHANGE, TEACHER_CHANGE, SPECIAL_EVENT, EXAM\n- Exception approval workflow: `PENDING` → `APPROVED`/`REJECTED` with audit trail\n- Recurring exception patterns (e.g., \"every Monday for 4 weeks\")\n- Substitute teacher assignment on exception approval\n- Student view (personal timetable), Teacher view (weekly schedule), Admin view (department oversight)\n- IST timezone enforcement with working-day configuration per academic calendar\n\n### Business Value\n- Reduces scheduling conflicts and manual coordination overhead\n- Enables real-time communication of timetable changes to affected stakeholders\n- Supports NAAC accreditation requirements for documented academic planning\n- Preserves historical timetable state for attendance session integrity\n\n### India-Specific Considerations\n- Supports dual-semester system (Odd/Even) and trimester variants\n- Accommodates regional holiday calendars (state-specific + national)\n- Handles split-shift colleges (morning/evening batches) common in urban India\n- Room allocation respects infrastructure constraints (lab availability, projector rooms)\n\n### MVP Status\n✅ **Production-Ready** — Core functionality built; notification wiring pending\n\n### Dependencies\n- Department, Course, Subject, Teacher, Room master data\n- Notification system for exception alerts\n- Attendance module (slot snapshot reference)\n\n### Acceptance Criteria\n- [ ] HOD can create/publish timetable for own department only\n- [ ] Exception approval triggers notification to affected students/teachers\n- [ ] Published timetable is read-only; changes require new exception request\n- [ ] Student/teacher views respect college isolation and role permissions\n- [ ] Timetable data is preserved in attendance sessions at time of creation\n\n---\n\n## 2️⃣ Teacher Lecture Report Module *(formerly \"Teacher Attendance\")*\n\n### Description\nA reporting module that tracks and aggregates teaching delivery data per teacher — capturing lecture sessions conducted, attendance taken, and delivery metrics. **Note**: This is not teacher presence tracking.\n\n### Key Features\n- Generates report of all closed attendance sessions conducted by a teacher\n- Metrics: total sessions, present count, absent count, delivery percentage\n- Filterable by date range, course, semester, department\n- Export to PDF/CSV for NAAC documentation and performance reviews\n- Integrated with timetable: only scheduled slots appear as \"expected sessions\"\n\n### Business Value\n- Provides data for teacher performance evaluation and workload analysis\n- Supports NAAC Criterion III (Teaching-Learning Processes) documentation\n- Enables data-driven decisions for faculty allocation and training needs\n\n### India-Specific Considerations\n- Accounts for guest faculty, visiting professors, and part-time instructors\n- Handles multi-campus teaching assignments common in affiliated colleges\n- Supports regional language labels for report exports (Hindi, Marathi, etc.)\n\n### MVP Status\n⚠️ **Partial** — Reporting logic built; naming clarification and UI polish needed\n\n### Dependencies\n- Attendance module (session data)\n- Timetable module (expected session baseline)\n- Teacher master data with department mapping\n\n### Acceptance Criteria\n- [ ] Report accurately reflects only closed, validated attendance sessions\n- [ ] Filters respect role-based data access (HOD sees dept only, Principal sees college-wide)\n- [ ] Exported reports include college header, date range, and authorized signatory placeholder\n- [ ] Module is clearly labeled \"Teacher Lecture Report\" to avoid confusion with presence tracking\n\n> 📌 **Future Enhancement (V1.2)**: Separate `TeacherPresence` module for daily attendance marking by admin/principal for salary and compliance.\n\n---\n\n## 3️⃣ Student Promotion & Alumni Management Module\n\n### Description\nA lifecycle management system for progressing students between academic years/semesters, with fee compliance checks and alumni transition handling.\n\n### Key Features\n- `PromotionHistory` model: tracks from/to semester, academic year, fee status, approver, remarks\n- Individual and bulk promotion workflows with eligibility filtering\n- Fee status validation at promotion time: `FULLY_PAID` / `PARTIALLY_PAID` / `PENDING`\n- Final-semester promotion auto-triggers `ALUMNI` status transition\n- Reversible promotion with audit trail (for correction scenarios)\n- Student model fields: `currentSemester`, `currentAcademicYear`, `isPromotionEligible`, `promotionHistory[]`\n\n### Business Value\n- Enforces institutional policy: no promotion with pending dues\n- Reduces manual errors in year-end student progression\n- Creates clean alumni data for placement, fundraising, and accreditation reporting\n- Supports reversal for administrative corrections without data loss\n\n### India-Specific Considerations\n- Handles academic year cycles (June–May) distinct from calendar year\n- Supports category-based fee waivers (SC/ST/OBC/EWS) in promotion eligibility logic\n- Alumni data retention complies with DPDPA consent requirements\n\n### MVP Status\n✅ **Solid** — Core logic built; notification and bulk override enhancements pending\n\n### Dependencies\n- Student fee module (fee status validation)\n- Academic calendar configuration\n- Notification system (promotion confirmation)\n\n### Acceptance Criteria\n- [ ] Bulk promotion respects fee status filter; admin can override with justification logging\n- [ ] Promotion triggers status update to `ALUMNI` for final-semester students\n- [ ] Reversal restores original semester/year and fee status accurately\n- [ ] Promotion confirmation email sent to student (and parent if linked)\n- [ ] Audit log captures who promoted, when, and any fee override remarks\n\n---\n\n## 4️⃣ Installment-Based Fee Payment Module\n\n### Description\nA flexible fee collection system supporting category-based fee structures, multi-installment plans, and atomic payment processing with race-condition protection.\n\n### Key Features\n- `FeeStructure` defined per college + course + category (GEN/OBC/SC/ST/EWS)\n- Installment array: name, amount, due date, late fee rules (configurable)\n- `StudentFee` mirrors structure per student; tracks status per installment: `PENDING`/`PAID`/`FAILED`/`CANCELLED`\n- Atomic update pattern: `updateOne` with `status: \"PENDING\"` condition to prevent double-payment\n- Duplicate payment protection: status check + unique payment ID validation\n- Payment mode tracking: ONLINE/CASH/CHEQUE/DD with reference number and remarks\n\n### Business Value\n- Aligns with Indian college practice of term-wise or monthly fee collection\n- Reduces revenue leakage from payment race conditions or manual errors\n- Supports scholarship disbursement tracking via category-based fee differentiation\n- Enables automated due-date reminders and late fee calculation\n\n### India-Specific Considerations\n- Category-based fee structures mandated by state governments for reserved categories\n- Supports installment plans aligned with academic terms (not calendar months)\n- Late fee logic configurable as % or fixed amount per state/university norms\n- Razorpay integration for UPI, Indian cards, net banking (primary); Stripe optional for NRI\n\n### MVP Status\n✅ **Solid** — Core payment logic built; due-date enforcement and reminder cron pending\n\n### Dependencies\n- Student enrollment and course assignment\n- Payment gateway integration (Razorpay primary)\n- Notification system for due-date reminders\n\n### Acceptance Criteria\n- [ ] Installments enforce sequential payment order (configurable per college)\n- [ ] Late fee auto-applies after due date based on college-configured rules\n- [ ] Atomic update prevents duplicate payment processing under concurrent requests\n- [ ] Payment status updates reflect in student dashboard and accountant reports in real-time\n- [ ] Offline payments (cash/cheque/DD) recorded with admin audit trail and reference number\n\n---\n\n## 5️⃣ Offline Payment Recording & Receipt Module\n\n### Description\nA workflow for recording and reconciling offline fee payments (cash, cheque, demand draft) with audit trail and official receipt generation.\n\n### Key Features\n- Admin can mark installment as paid offline with: payment mode, reference number, remarks\n- Full audit trail: which admin recorded, timestamp, IP address\n- Receipt generation: PDF with college branding, payment details, authorized signatory placeholder\n- Receipt delivery: email to student + parent (if linked) + download from dashboard\n- Reconciliation support: reference number search, batch upload for bulk cheque/DD processing\n\n### Business Value\n- Critical for Indian colleges where >60% of fee payments are offline (RBI data)\n- Reduces reconciliation errors and disputes through structured recording\n- Provides auditable trail for internal finance teams and external auditors\n- Enhances parent/student trust with immediate official receipt\n\n### India-Specific Considerations\n- Supports DD/cheque number formats used by Indian banks\n- Receipt includes mandatory fields per Indian accounting standards: date, amount in words, GST breakdown if applicable\n- Cash payments require dual-approval workflow for amounts above threshold (configurable)\n\n### MVP Status\n✅ **Complete** — Recording logic built; receipt PDF generation pending\n\n### Dependencies\n- Student fee module (installment status update)\n- PDF generation service\n- Email/notification system for receipt delivery\n\n### Acceptance Criteria\n- [ ] Offline payment recording updates installment status to `PAID` with mode and reference\n- [ ] Receipt PDF includes: college name/address, student details, payment breakdown, reference number, timestamp, admin name\n- [ ] Receipt is emailed to student and parent within 5 minutes of recording\n- [ ] Admin can re-download or re-send receipt from payment history\n- [ ] Audit log captures all offline payment modifications with before/after values\n\n---\n\n## 6️⃣ Payment Gateway Integration Module (Razorpay Primary)\n\n### Description\nA pluggable payment gateway architecture supporting per-college configuration, encrypted credential storage, and webhook handling for payment confirmation.\n\n### Key Features\n- `CollegePaymentConfig` model: per-college gateway selection (Razorpay/Stripe), encrypted credentials\n- Credential encryption: AES-256-GCM with PBKDF2 key derivation\n- In-memory caching of gateway instances (5-min TTL) for performance\n- Webhook handlers for payment success/failure/refund events\n- Admin UI for college admins to configure gateway keys (with role-based access)\n- Fallback logic: if primary gateway fails, queue for retry with alert\n\n### Business Value\n- Enables colleges to use their own merchant accounts (required for GST invoicing)\n- Reduces platform liability by not handling raw card data\n- Supports multi-gateway strategy for redundancy and regional optimization\n- Webhook-driven confirmation ensures payment status accuracy without polling\n\n### India-Specific Considerations\n- Razorpay prioritized for MVP: supports UPI, RuPay, Indian net banking, EMI options\n- Stripe retained for NRI/international student payments (optional, hidden by default)\n- Webhook endpoints comply with RBI guidelines for payment confirmation latency\n- GST-compliant transaction metadata passed to gateway for invoice reconciliation\n\n### MVP Status\n✅ **Built** — Architecture sound; Stripe deprecation decision pending for India MVP\n\n### Dependencies\n- College model (for config storage)\n- Student fee module (payment status update)\n- Notification system (payment confirmation alerts)\n\n### Acceptance Criteria\n- [ ] College admin can configure Razorpay keys via secure UI; credentials stored encrypted\n- [ ] Payment initiation redirects to gateway with college-specific merchant ID\n- [ ] Webhook handler validates signature, updates payment status, triggers receipt generation\n- [ ] Failed payments show clear error with retry option; no duplicate charges\n- [ ] Stripe integration is feature-flagged and hidden from India-targeted colleges by default\n\n---\n\n## 7️⃣ Configurable Document Requirements Module\n\n### Description\nA dynamic form configuration system allowing colleges to define mandatory/optional document requirements for student registration, with validation rules and category-based conditional logic.\n\n### Key Features\n- `DocumentConfig` model: per-college, per-collegeCode list of document types\n- Per-document settings: enabled/disabled, mandatory flag, allowed formats, max size (1-20MB), description, display order\n- 18 supported document types: 10th/12th marksheet, passport photo, category certificate, income certificate, character certificate, transfer certificate, Aadhaar, entrance score, migration certificate, domicile, caste, non-creamy layer, PwD, sports quota, NRI sponsor, gap certificate, affidavit\n- Dynamic validation during student registration: checks config, enforces mandatory fields, skips category-inapplicable docs (e.g., caste certificate for GEN)\n- File upload with format/size validation and virus scanning\n\n### Business Value\n- Eliminates hard-coded document logic; adapts to varied institution types (arts/science/engineering/medical)\n- Reduces application rejection due to missing documents through clear, college-specific guidance\n- Supports compliance with state/university admission guidelines that vary by region and program\n- Enables rapid onboarding of new college tenants without code changes\n\n### India-Specific Considerations\n- Category certificate logic auto-skips for GEN students (per UGC norms)\n- Supports regional document names (e.g., \"Domicile\" vs \"Residence Certificate\")\n- Aadhaar upload optional with explicit consent per DPDPA; never made mandatory unless legally required\n- File size limits aligned with common Indian broadband upload capabilities\n\n### MVP Status\n✅ **Impressive** — Validation logic built; admin UI and config versioning pending\n\n### Dependencies\n- Student registration workflow\n- File storage service (S3-compatible)\n- Notification system (document submission confirmation)\n\n### Acceptance Criteria\n- [ ] Admin can enable/disable document types, set mandatory flag, allowed formats, max size via UI\n- [ ] Student registration form dynamically renders fields based on college config and student category\n- [ ] Upload validation rejects disallowed formats/sizes with clear error messages\n- [ ] Category-based conditional logic correctly skips inapplicable documents (e.g., caste cert for GEN)\n- [ ] Config changes are versioned; students who submitted under prior config are not forced to re-upload\n\n---\n\n## 8️⃣ HOD Role & Permission Overlay Module\n\n### Description\nA permission-layer implementation where Head of Department (HOD) is not a standalone role but an elevated permission set applied to a TEACHER, scoped to department-level timetable and approval workflows.\n\n### Key Features\n- HOD assigned via `Department.hod_id` reference to a Teacher record\n- `hod.middleware.js`: validates requesting teacher is HOD of target department\n- Permissions: create/edit/publish timetables for own department; manage slots; approve timetable exceptions\n- UI: `AssignHod.jsx` for admin to designate HOD per department\n- Permission resolution: primary role (TEACHER) + secondary overlay (HOD) merged at runtime\n\n### Business Value\n- Avoids role explosion in enum; HOD is a responsibility, not a distinct job title\n- Enables fine-grained departmental autonomy without compromising college-wide data isolation\n- Supports Indian college hierarchy where HODs have operational authority within departments\n- Simplifies user management: one user account with multiple permission layers\n\n### India-Specific Considerations\n- Aligns with UGC/AICTE norms where HOD is a faculty member with added administrative duties\n- Supports multi-HOD scenarios (e.g., separate HOD for UG/PG in same department)\n- Department scoping respects university affiliation boundaries (e.g., autonomous vs affiliated colleges)\n\n### MVP Status\n✅ **Clean Design** — Timetable permissions built; expansion to leave approval/reports pending\n\n### Dependencies\n- Department model with `hod_id` field\n- Timetable module (primary use case)\n- Permission middleware (hybrid architecture)\n\n### Acceptance Criteria\n- [ ] Only assigned HOD can create/edit/publish timetables for their department\n- [ ] HOD permissions are scoped strictly to own department; no cross-department access\n- [ ] Admin can reassign HOD; historical timetables retain original approver audit trail\n- [ ] HOD can approve timetable exceptions for their department only\n- [ ] Permission overlay is resolved at runtime; no enum changes required for HOD functionality\n\n> 📌 **Future Enhancement (V1.1)**: Expand HOD permissions to include leave approval, department reports, budget oversight.\n\n---\n\n## 9️⃣ Notification System Module\n\n### Description\nA college-scoped, multi-target broadcast system for in-app notifications with read-tracking, granular audience selection, and action deep-linking.\n\n### Key Features\n- `Notification` model: college-scoped, 8 types (GENERAL, ACADEMIC, EXAM, FEE, ATTENDANCE, EVENT, ASSIGNMENT, URGENT)\n- 7 targeting options: ALL, STUDENTS, TEACHERS, DEPARTMENT, COURSE, SEMESTER, INDIVIDUAL\n- `NotificationRead` model: separate read-status tracking per user (avoids broadcast bloat)\n- Unread count API per role for badge display\n- `actionUrl` field for deep-linking to relevant module (e.g., fee due → payment page)\n- `expiresAt` field for time-bound notifications (e.g., exam reminders)\n\n### Business Value\n- Reduces email overload by prioritizing in-app delivery for operational alerts\n- Enables targeted communication (e.g., \"Semester 3 CS students only\") without manual filtering\n- Supports compliance: URGENT notifications for exam schedule changes, fee deadlines\n- Read-tracking provides engagement metrics for admin communication effectiveness\n\n### India-Specific Considerations\n- In-app primary delivery accounts for low-email-engagement among students/parents in tier-2/3 cities\n- URGENT type triggers SMS fallback (via integration) for critical alerts (exam cancellation, fee deadline)\n- Regional language support in notification content (Hindi, Marathi, Tamil, etc.)\n\n### MVP Status\n✅ **Well-Designed** — Core model and APIs built; email trigger and expiry enforcement pending\n\n### Dependencies\n- User model with role/department/course/semester metadata\n- Frontend routing for `actionUrl` deep-linking\n- Email/SMS service for fallback channels\n\n### Acceptance Criteria\n- [ ] Admin/teacher can create notification with type, target audience, content, actionUrl, expiry\n- [ ] Targeted notifications delivered only to matching users (e.g., DEPARTMENT + CS → only CS dept users)\n- [ ] Read status tracked per user; unread count updates in real-time\n- [ ] `actionUrl` correctly routes user to target module when notification clicked\n- [ ] Expired notifications auto-archive and no longer appear in active feeds\n\n---\n\n## 🔟 Institutional Subscription & Billing Module\n\n### Description\nA tender-aware, offline-payment-first billing workflow for Indian educational institutions, managed by SUPER_ADMIN with college-level payment proof submission and verification.\n\n### Key Features\n- **Invoice Generation**: SUPER_ADMIN creates invoice with college details, plan, GST breakdown, due date, payment instructions, QR code\n- **Multi-Recipient Delivery**: Invoice sent to COLLEGE_ADMIN (primary) + PRINCIPAL/REGISTRAR (secondary) + billing contact email\n- **Offline Payment Workflow**: College pays via bank transfer/DD/cheque; uploads proof (scanned copy, UTR/DD number) via portal\n- **Verification & Activation**: SUPER_ADMIN reviews proof, matches with bank statement, approves → extends `subscriptionExpiry`, sends receipt\n- **Grace Period Handling**: Configurable grace days for tender delays; read-only mode at expiry, hard block after grace period\n- **Audit & Compliance**: Full audit log for invoice creation, proof upload, approval; GST-compliant receipt generation\n\n### Business Value\n- Aligns with Indian institutional procurement: tenders, purchase orders, offline payments\n- Reduces churn from payment friction by supporting college-preferred payment methods\n- Ensures revenue recognition through verified payment proof before service continuation\n- Supports DPDPA compliance via explicit billing data consent and audit trails\n\n### India-Specific Considerations\n- Tender reference field for government college procurement tracking\n- Purchase order (PO) upload support before invoice generation\n- Financial year-aligned invoicing (Apr 1 – Mar 31) with academic year renewal options\n- GST-compliant invoice format: CGST/SGST for intra-state, IGST for inter-state\n- Multi-signatory approval workflow for government colleges (PRINCIPAL + ACCOUNTANT co-sign)\n\n### MVP Status\n❌ **Half-Built** — Middleware enforcement exists; data model and UI missing\n\n### Dependencies\n- College model extensions (`subscriptionPlan`, `subscriptionExpiry`, `billingContact*`, `gstNumber`)\n- Invoice model (new entity)\n- Notification system for billing alerts\n- PDF generation for invoice/receipt\n\n### Acceptance Criteria\n- [ ] SUPER_ADMIN can create invoice with college, plan, amounts, GST, due date, payment instructions\n- [ ] Invoice PDF generated with mandatory Indian compliance fields (GSTIN, QR code, financial year)\n- [ ] COLLEGE_ADMIN/PRINCIPAL can upload payment proof against outstanding invoice\n- [ ] SUPER_ADMIN can review proof, approve/reject with comments; approval triggers subscription extension\n- [ ] Receipt PDF generated on approval; emailed to college contacts; available for download\n- [ ] Grace period logic: warning at -7 days, read-only at expiry, block after grace; configurable per college\n- [ ] Audit log captures all billing actions with actor, timestamp, IP, invoice ID, proof reference\n\n---\n\n## 1️⃣1️⃣ Soft Delete & Cascade Deactivation Module\n\n### Description\nA data lifecycle management system enabling college-level deactivation with cascading soft-delete across 14+ related collections, and safe restoration with status preservation.\n\n### Key Features\n- `College.isActive` flag as master switch for tenant availability\n- Cascade soft-delete: deactivating college sets `isActive: false` on related records in: departments, courses, students, teachers, subjects, fee structures, student fees, notifications, timetables, slots, attendance sessions, records, document configs, users\n- Cascade restore: reactivating college restores related records **with original statuses preserved** (not forced to APPROVED)\n- Hard delete option: permanent removal of college and all related data (with confirmation workflow)\n- Student/Teacher/User deactivation: independent status flags (`DEACTIVATED`, `INACTIVE`, `isActive: false`) for individual lifecycle management\n\n### Business Value\n- Enables safe tenant offboarding without data loss; supports reactivation if college renews\n- Prevents orphaned data and referential integrity issues during deactivation\n- Supports compliance: DPDPA right-to-erasure via hard delete workflow with audit\n- Reduces support overhead: one-click deactivation vs manual record-by-record updates\n\n### India-Specific Considerations\n- Student status preservation on restore critical for academic continuity (e.g., REJECTED students must not become APPROVED)\n- Hard delete workflow includes DPDPA-mandated confirmation: \"This action permanently erases all personal data; cannot be undone\"\n- Audit logs retain deactivation/reactivation events for compliance reporting even after data purge\n\n### MVP Status\n✅ **Thorough** — Cascade logic built; restore bug and hook consolidation pending\n\n### Dependencies\n- Mongoose pre-hooks for `findOneAndUpdate` and `findOneAndDelete`\n- Audit logging system for deactivation events\n- Backup/restore infrastructure for hard delete scenarios\n\n### Acceptance Criteria\n- [ ] Deactivating college sets `isActive: false` on all related collections; data remains queryable with `isActive` filter\n- [ ] Restoring college reactivates related records **with original statuses** (APPROVED stays APPROVED, REJECTED stays REJECTED)\n- [ ] Duplicate pre-hooks merged into single hook with conditional logic to prevent conflicting executions\n- [ ] Hard delete requires SUPER_ADMIN confirmation + audit log entry; permanently removes data per DPDPA\n- [ ] Individual student/teacher deactivation works independently of college status; respects role permissions\n\n---\n\n## 📊 Module Priority Matrix for PRD\n\n| Module | MVP Criticality | Effort | Risk if Deferred | Recommended 📋 Revised Module: Student Promotion & Academic Progression\n\n> **PRD Ready | India-Compliant | No Code | Focus: ATKT, Grace, Roundoff, Year-Down, Conditional Fee Logic**\n\n---\n\n## 🔍 Core Problem Identified\nThe previous promotion logic assumed a binary `PASS → PROMOTE` flow gated by fee clearance. This does **not reflect Indian university ordinances**, where promotion is governed by:\n- Subject-wise pass/fail thresholds\n- Backlog limits (ATKT)\n- Grace mark & roundoff policies\n- Year-down/detention rules\n- Conditional fee holds vs academic progression\n\nIndian colleges separate **academic progression** from **financial clearance**. A student can be academically promoted with pending fees (result/transcript withheld), or year-down despite full fee payment due to backlogs.\n\n---\n\n## 🎯 Corrected Module Scope\n\n### 1. Academic Progression Engine\nReplaces manual \"promote\" toggle with a rule-driven calculation that evaluates:\n- **Subject-wise performance**: Internal + external marks vs pass threshold\n- **Backlog count**: Number of failed/absent subjects\n- **ATKT eligibility**: University-configured backlog limit for conditional progression\n- **Grace mark application**: Pre-pass calculation (1–2 marks/subject, max 1–2/semester per ordinance)\n- **Roundoff policy**: Applied before pass/fail determination (e.g., ≥0.5 rounds up)\n- **Fee status**: Soft-block (result withheld) vs hard-block (promotion denied)\n\n### 2. Promotion Decision Outcomes\n| Outcome | Trigger | Academic Status | Fee Status | Next Action |\n|---------|---------|----------------|------------|-------------|\n| `PROMOTED` | All subjects passed, within norms | Cleared | Cleared or conditional | Advance to next semester/year |\n| `ATKT_PROMOTED` | Failed subjects ≤ ATKT limit | Backlog carry | Cleared or conditional | Advance with backlog subjects flagged |\n| `YEAR_DOWN` | Failed subjects > ATKT limit or mandatory repeat subjects | Detained | Cleared | Repeat semester/year; no progression |\n| `RESULT_WITHHELD` | Academically cleared but fees pending | Cleared | PENDING | Progression allowed, degree/transcript blocked |\n| `ALUMNI` | Final year cleared, no pending backlogs, fees cleared | Graduated | Cleared | Alumni status, degree eligibility |\n\n### 3. Configurable University Ordinances (Per College)\nColleges must configure rules matching their affiliating university:\n- `ATKT_LIMIT`: Max backlogs allowed for conditional promotion (e.g., 2, 3, or 4)\n- `GRACE_POLICY`: Marks per subject (1–2), max per semester, eligibility (only for borderline fail)\n- `ROUNDOFF_RULE`: Threshold for upward rounding (e.g., `≥0.5`, `≥0.75`, or disabled)\n- `PASS_CRITERIA`: Per subject (e.g., 40%), aggregate (e.g., 50%), internal/external split\n- `FEE_PROMOTION_POLICY`: `ALLOW_WITH_HOLD`, `BLOCK_IF_PENDING`, `IGNORE`\n- `YEAR_DOWN_TRIGGERS`: Mandatory repeat subjects, attendance shortfall, backlog expiry\n\n### 4. Workflow Sequence\n```\n1. Marks Entry (Internal + External) → Locked by HOD/Principal\n2. System applies Roundoff → then Grace Marks → then calculates Pass/Fail per subject\n3. Counts backlogs → checks ATKT limit → determines progression outcome\n4. Checks fee status → applies soft/hold policy if configured\n5. Generates PromotionDecision record with:\n   • Outcome status\n   • Subject-wise breakdown (pass/fail/grace applied)\n   • Backlog list (if ATKT)\n   • Fee clearance status\n   • Approver + timestamp\n6. Updates Student academic record:\n   • currentSemester/currentYear\n   • backlogCount[]\n   • promotionStatus\n7. Triggers notifications:\n   • Student/Parent: Result + next steps\n   • Accountant: Fee hold status (if applicable)\n   • HOD/Principal: ATKT/Year-down list for academic counseling\n```\n\n### 5. Data Model Adjustments (Conceptual)\n- Replace flat `PromotionHistory` with `AcademicProgressionRecord`:\n  - `student_id`, `academic_year`, `semester_from`, `semester_to`\n  - `outcome`: enum [PROMOTED, ATKT_PROMOTED, YEAR_DOWN, RESULT_WITHHELD, ALUMNI]\n  - `subject_results[]`: subject, internal, external, total, pass_status, grace_applied, roundoff_applied\n  - `backlog_count`, `atkt_eligible`, `fee_clearance_status`\n  - `approved_by`, `approved_at`, `override_justification` (for manual corrections)\n- `UniversityOrdinanceConfig` (per college): stores ATKT, grace, roundoff, pass criteria, fee policy\n\n### 6. Manual Override & Audit\n- Principal/HOD can override system decision with mandatory justification\n- Override does not recalculate marks; only changes outcome status (e.g., `YEAR_DOWN → ATKT_PROMOTED` for medical/compassionate grounds)\n- Full audit trail: original calculation, override reason, approver, timestamp, IP\n- Overrides limited to 1 per academic cycle per student (configurable)\n\n### 7. India-Specific Compliance Notes\n- Aligns with UGC CBCS, affiliated university ordinances, and state HE guidelines\n- Grace/roundoff applied **before** pass/fail determination (as per university norms)\n- ATKT backlog carry limited to 2 academic years (system auto-blocks promotion if backlog age exceeds limit)\n- Fee holds comply with UGC directive: cannot deny academic progression solely on fee grounds; can withhold degree/transcript\n- Supports regional academic calendars (June–May, Apr–Mar, trimester variants)\n\n---\n\n## ✅ PRD Acceptance Criteria\n\n| Criteria | Validation Method |\n|----------|------------------|\n| Roundoff applied before pass/fail calculation | Test with 39.5, 39.4, 40.0 marks; verify pass status |\n| Grace marks applied only to borderline fails | Test with 38, 39, 40 marks; verify 1-mark grace triggers pass only if ≤ threshold |\n| ATKT limit enforces conditional progression | Configure limit=2; test with 1, 2, 3 backlogs; verify outcomes |\n| Year-down triggers correctly when backlog limit exceeded | Verify system blocks progression and flags repeat semester |\n| Fee hold allows academic progression but blocks degree/transcript | Test with pending fees; verify student advances but transcript status = WITHHELD |\n| Manual override requires justification and logs audit | Test override flow; verify audit trail captures reason, approver, timestamp |\n| Backlog age limit prevents indefinite ATKT carry | Test with backlog from 3 years ago; verify auto-block to YEAR_DOWN |\n| Notifications trigger for all outcomes | Verify student, parent, accountant, HOD receive correct alerts |\n| Configurable ordinance applies per college | Test two colleges with different ATKT/grace rules; verify independent evaluation |\n\n---\n\n## 📅 MVP vs V1.1 Scope\n\n| Feature | MVP | V1.1 |\n|--------|-----|------|\n| Subject-wise pass/fail calculation | ✅ | — |\n| Roundoff & grace mark engine | ✅ | Advanced grace rules (aggregate vs subject-wise) |\n| ATKT limit enforcement | ✅ | Backlog expiry tracking (2-year rule) |\n| Fee conditional hold | ✅ | Partial fee release workflows |\n| Manual override with audit | ✅ | Multi-level approval (HOD → Principal → Super Admin) |\n| Year-down automation | ✅ | Re-admission workflow for detained students |\n| Ordinance config per college | ✅ | University template library (MU, PU, DU, etc.) |\n| Transcript/degree block on fee hold | ✅ | Integration with alumni portal for degree release |\n\n---\n\n## 🚨 Critical PRD Notes for Engineering & QA\n1. **Promotion is no longer a button** — it's a calculated outcome triggered after marks finalization and ordinance evaluation.\n2. **Grace & roundoff are pre-pass modifiers** — never applied after fail determination.\n3. **Fee status ≠ academic status** — system must decouple progression from financial clearance per UGC guidelines.\n4. **ATKT is a backlog count, not a mark adjustment** — carry-backlog subjects remain in student record until cleared.\n5. **Year-down is irreversible without override** — system must prevent accidental promotion of detained students.\n\n---\n\n> 💡 **PRD Integration Tip**: Replace the old `Student Promotion/Alumni` section entirely with this revised spec. 📚 Indian University Student Pass/Fail & Promotion Logic — Comprehensive Research\n\n> **Purpose**: PRD-ready specification reflecting actual Indian higher education ordinances, UGC CBCS guidelines, and state university practices.  \n> **Scope**: Evaluation thresholds, grace/roundoff, ATKT/conditional promotion, detention/year-down, backlog clearance, fee vs academic decoupling, and configurable rule engines.  \n> **Compliance Base**: UGC Regulations (CBCS), AICTE/State HE Department Guidelines, Supreme Court/UGC rulings on fee-academic separation.\n\n---\n\n## 🔍 1. Evaluation Framework & Multi-Threshold Passing Logic\n\nIndian universities **rarely use a single \"pass mark\"**. Passing is a multi-layered check:\n\n| Threshold | Typical Requirement | Notes |\n|-----------|---------------------|-------|\n| **Internal Assessment (IA)** | ≥ 35–40% of IA marks | Continuous assessment, assignments, tests |\n| **External/End-Semester (ESE)** | ≥ 40–50% of ESE marks | University-conducted final exam |\n| **Aggregate (IA + ESE)** | ≥ 40–50% of total | Must pass both component & aggregate |\n| **Practical/Project** | ≥ 40% + separate viva | Often independent pass/fail |\n| **Attendance** | ≥ 75% (condonable to 60–65%) | Medical/extra-curricular condonation rules apply |\n| **Credit Completion** | Min SGPA/CGPA ≥ 4.0 (P grade) | CBCS credit-weighted calculation |\n\n**Key Rule**: `PASS = ALL thresholds met`. Failing ANY single component results in `F` grade for that subject, even if aggregate is above passing.\n\n---\n\n## 🎯 2. Grace Marks & Roundoff Mechanics\n\n### Grace Marks\n| Parameter | Standard Practice | Constraints |\n|-----------|-------------------|-------------|\n| **Eligibility** | Borderline failures (1–2 marks below pass) | Only for theory subjects; not for practicals, core engineering/medical subjects, or if >2 subjects failed |\n| **Quantum** | 1–2 marks per subject | Max 1–2 per semester; cannot upgrade grade beyond `P` |\n| **Application** | Auto-applied post-result declaration | Requires audit log; some universities require student application + HOD recommendation |\n| **UGC Restriction** | Prohibited in professional courses (Engg, Med, Law, Pharmacy) for core subjects | Must be configurable per course type |\n\n### Roundoff\n| Level | Practice | Notes |\n|-------|----------|-------|\n| **Subject Marks** | Rarely rounded | Most universities use exact marks for pass/fail determination |\n| **SGPA/CGPA** | Rounded to 2 decimal places | Standard across CBCS universities |\n| **Sequence** | Component check → Aggregate → CGPA calculation → Roundoff → Grace → Final Grade | Grace is applied **after** roundoff, only to remaining borderline fails |\n\n---\n\n## 🔄 3. ATKT / Conditional Promotion (Backlog Rules)\n\n**ATKT** = *Allowed To Keep Terms* (legacy term; now officially `Conditional Promotion` or `Backlog Promotion`).\n\n| Rule | Typical Practice | Variations |\n|------|------------------|------------|\n| **Eligibility** | Failed subjects ≤ N | UG: 2–3, PG: 1–2, Professional: 0–1 |\n| **Promotion Type** | Conditional progression to next semester | Backlogs remain active; must clear within 2–3 academic years |\n| **Exam Fee** | Additional backlog paper fee per subject | Collected at re-exam registration |\n| **Attendance** | May be relaxed for backlog re-exams | Some universities allow 50% min for backlog papers |\n| **Final Year Restriction** | ATKT not allowed in final semester/year | All backlogs must be cleared before appearing for final exams |\n| **Backlog Age Limit** | Max 2–3 years to clear | Older backlogs auto-trigger detention/year-down |\n\n**System Logic**:  \n`IF backlog_count ≤ ATKT_limit AND not_final_semester → PROMOTE_CONDITIONALLY`  \n`ELSE → DETAIN / YEAR_DOWN`\n\n---\n\n## 📉 4. Year-Down / Detention / Academic Probation\n\nIn semester systems, \"year-down\" is a misnomer. Correct terms: `Semester Detention`, `Repeat Semester`, or `Academic Detention`.\n\n| Trigger | University Practice | System Action |\n|---------|---------------------|---------------|\n| **Exceed ATKT limit** | > allowed backlogs | Detain to current semester; re-register |\n| **Attendance < 75%** | Without condonation approval | Block exam eligibility; repeat semester |\n| **Max Attempts Exhausted** | Usually 3–4 attempts per subject (incl. re-exams) | Subject deemed failed; may require course change or exit with diploma |\n| **Malpractice/Disciplinary** | As per university ordinance | Suspend/hold results; manual override required |\n| **Backlog Age Expiry** | Backlogs older than 2–3 years | Auto-detention; re-admission workflow triggered |\n\n**Probation Policy**:  \n- First detention → `Academic Probation` status  \n- Second consecutive detention → Mandatory counseling, parent notification, potential course exit option  \n- Probation students eligible for promotion only after clearing all backlogs\n\n---\n\n## 📖 5. Backlog Clearance & Grade Replacement\n\n| Aspect | Standard Practice |\n|--------|-------------------|\n| **Re-Exam Schedule** | After each semester or annual cycle; concurrent with regular exams |\n| **Grade Policy** | `F` replaced with new grade, but often capped (e.g., max `B` or `P` for backlog clearance) |\n| **Transcript Annotation** | Some universities mark `*` or `B` (backlog cleared) on transcript |\n| **Attempt Count** | Tracked per subject; displayed in student academic record |\n| **Concurrent Clearing** | Students can clear up to N backlogs while studying current semester (varies by university) |\n\n---\n\n## 💰 6. Fee vs Academic Progression (UGC Mandate)\n\n**UGC Directive (2020/2023)**: *Academic progression and exam eligibility cannot be blocked solely due to fee dues.*\n\n| Separation | Implementation |\n|------------|----------------|\n| `academic_status` | Determined purely by marks, attendance, backlog rules |\n| `financial_clearance` | Tracks fee payment; does not block promotion |\n| **Financial Hold** | Can withhold degree, transcript, bonafide, or placement eligibility |\n| **Exam Eligibility** | Must remain open if academically eligible, regardless of fee status |\n| **System Enforcement** | Decoupled flags: `promotion_allowed` vs `degree_release_allowed` |\n\n> ⚠️ Blocking promotion/exams for fee dues is **legally non-compliant** and has led to UGC penalties and court rulings against colleges.\n\n---\n\n## ⚙️ 7. Configurable University Ordinance Engine\n\nColleges must support **affiliate university-specific rules** without code changes.\n\n| Configurable Parameter | Example Values | Notes |\n|------------------------|----------------|-------|\n| `pass_internal_min` | 35, 40 | % of internal marks |\n| `pass_external_min` | 40, 45, 50 | % of external marks |\n| `pass_aggregate_min` | 40, 50 | Overall % |\n| `attendance_min` | 75 (condonable to 65) | With medical/committee approval |\n| `atkt_limit_ug` | 2, 3 | Max backlogs for conditional promotion |\n| `atkt_limit_pg` | 1, 2 | |\n| `grace_marks_per_subject` | 0, 1, 2 | Max 0 for professional cores |\n| `grace_semester_cap` | 1, 2 | Total grace per sem |\n| `max_attempts_per_subject` | 3, 4 | Incl. regular + re-exams |\n| `backlog_clearance_years` | 2, 3 | Max duration to clear |\n| `grade_capping_backlog` | `P`, `B`, `none` | Max grade for cleared backlog |\n| `fee_promotion_policy` | `ALLOW`, `HOLD_DEGREE`, `IGNORE` | UGC-compliant separation |\n\n**Rule Evaluation Sequence**:\n1. Validate attendance → condone if approved\n2. Check component minimums (IA, ESE, Practical)\n3. Calculate aggregate & SGPA/CGPA\n4. Apply roundoff (CGPA level)\n5. Apply grace marks (borderline fails only)\n6. Determine pass/fail per subject\n7. Count backlogs → check ATKT limit\n8. Apply fee policy (decoupled from academic status)\n9. Generate outcome: `PROMOTED`, `ATKT_PROMOTED`, `DETAINED`, `RESULT_WITHHELD`, `ALUMNI`\n\n---\n\n## 🌍 8. Real-World University Variations (Examples)\n\n| University | Pass Criteria | ATKT | Grace | Attendance | Notes |\n|------------|---------------|------|-------|------------|-------|\n| **Mumbai University** | 40% aggregate, 35% IA, 40% ESE | ≤2 backlogs | 2 marks/subject, max 2/sem | 75% (condonable) | Strict final-year clearance |\n| **Savitribai Phule Pune Univ.** | CBCS, SGPA ≥4.0 | ≤2 up to Sem V | 1 mark subject-wise | 75% | No ATKT in Sem VI/VIII |\n| **University of Delhi** | 35% min each component | None (strict) | Not permitted | 66.6% min | Backlogs must clear before next year |\n| **Anna University** | 50% pass (theory + practical) | ≤1 backlog | Not for core subjects | 75% | Strict grade capping on backlog |\n| **Calcutta University** | 40% aggregate, 30% IA, 40% ESE | ≤3 | 2 marks max | 70% | Condonation via medical board |\n\n> ✅ **System Requirement**: Ordinance profiles must be template-driven and assignable per college.\n\n---\n\n## ✅ 9. PRD Acceptance Criteria (Validation Checklist)\n\n| Scenario | Expected System Behavior |\n|----------|--------------------------|\n| Student scores 39.5 in ESE, pass=40, roundoff enabled | Rounds to 40 → Pass (if IA & aggregate met) |\n| Student scores 38, grace=2 allowed | Grace applied → 40 → Pass; logged with reason |\n| Student fails 3 subjects, ATKT limit=2 | `ATKT_PROMOTED` → backlogs flagged, next sem allowed |\n| Student fails 4 subjects, ATKT limit=2 | `DETAINED` → repeat semester, backlog age tracked |\n| Student has pending fees, academically cleared | `PROMOTED` + `DEGREE_WITHHELD` flag set |\n| Final year student with 1 backlog | Blocked from final exams; must clear backlog first |\n| Backlog older than 3 years | Auto-triggers detention/re-admission workflow |\n| Manual override applied | Requires justification, logs audit, caps to 1/cycle |\n| Professional course (B.Tech) with core subject fail | Grace marks blocked; only ATKT or detention options |\n\n---\n\n## 📌 10. Edge Cases & Compliance Notes\n\n| Edge Case | Handling |\n|-----------|----------|\n| **Medical condonation** | Requires document upload + Principal approval; system logs override reason |\n| **Lateral entry / credit transfer** | Maps to equivalent semester; backlog rules apply from entry point |\n| **Diploma exit** | If max attempts exhausted, system triggers diploma eligibility check |\n| **Malpractice case** | Results held; manual intervention required before progression |\n| **NRI/International student** | Same academic rules; fee policy may differ (configurable) |\n| **DPDPA compliance** | Academic records retained 5–10 years; anonymization after degree issuance |\n| **Audit trail** | Every pass/fail/grace/ATKT/override action logged with actor, timestamp, IP, ordinance version |\n\n---\n\n## 🗂️ PRD Integration Guidance\n\n1. **Replace** the old \"Student Promotion\" section with this spec.\n2. **Add** `UniversityOrdinanceConfig` as a core entity in your data model section.\n3. **Decouple** `academic_status` and `financial_clearance` in all role permission matrices.\n4. **Flag** UGC compliance notes for legal review before pilot launch.\n5. **Use** the acceptance criteria table directly for QA test case generation.\n\n> 💡 **Pro Tip**: Start with a `Mumbai University CBCS` and `Pune University CBCS` ordinance template as defaults. 70% of Maharashtra colleges align with these.
