Even today, done by hand.\"` | Digital generation + physical issuance tracking | Template engine, QR verification, issuance audit log, checklist for original document surrender |\n| `\"After 2nd year, student can change college. Physical originals while submission ensures not pursuing two degrees.\"` | Anti-fraud & double-enrollment prevention | Status locking (`ACTIVE → TRANSFERRED`), mandatory original surrender verification, inter-college validation placeholder |\n| `\"After final year, degree generation template. Autonomous colleges need it.\"` | Autonomous degree certificate engine | Configurable templates, batch generation, convocation workflow, university affiliation toggle |\n\n---\n\n## 📊 Module 1: Examination & Results Processing Module\n\n### Purpose\nProcess marks, apply university ordinances, calculate results, manage backlogs, and trigger academic progression. **Not an online exam platform** — a results & compliance engine.\n\n### Core Workflow\n```\n1. Marks Entry (Internal + External) → Locked by HOD/Principal\n2. Ordinance Engine Applies: Attendance validation → Component thresholds → Aggregate → Roundoff → Grace\n3. Pass/Fail Determination per subject → Backlog count → ATKT check → Final outcome\n4. Draft Results Published → Student/Parent portal preview (read-only)\n5. Approval by Principal → Official Result Publication\n6. System Triggers:\n   • Academic progression update\n   • Backlog list for re-exam registration\n   • Certificate eligibility checks (Degree/LC/TC)\n   • Financial hold evaluation (for document release, not progression)\n```\n\n### Key Features\n- **Configurable Ordinance Profiles**: Per-college templates matching affiliated university rules (pass thresholds, ATKT limits, grace/roundoff, attendance condonation)\n- **Result Outcomes**: `PASSED`, `ATKT_PROMOTED`, `DETAINED/YEAR_DOWN`, `RESULT_WITHHELD`, `FINAL_YEAR_CLEARED`\n- **Backlog Registry**: Tracks failed subjects, attempt count, age of backlog (auto-blocks if >2–3 years)\n- **Re-Exam Eligibility Engine**: Filters students eligible for backlog papers, generates fee challans, prevents double registration\n- **Transcript Generation**: Semester-wise mark sheets with grade points, credits, SGPA/CGPA, UGC CBCS compliant format\n- **Audit & Override**: Manual result correction requires Principal/HOD approval + justification log; caps at 1 override per academic cycle\n\n### Compliance & Indian Context\n- Aligns with UGC CBCS grading framework\n- Grace/roundoff applied **before** pass/fail determination\n- Academic progression **decoupled** from fee clearance (UGC mandate)\n- Professional course restrictions on grace marks enforced via ordinance config\n\n---\n\n## 📜 Module 2: Certificate Management (LC/TC & Degree)\n\n### Purpose\nDigitally generate, track, and securely issue Leaving Certificates (LC), Transfer Certificates (TC), and Degree Certificates. Bridges digital workflow with mandatory physical issuance and original document surrender.\n\n### A. LC / TC Generation Workflow\n\n| Stage | System Action | Compliance/Verification |\n|-------|---------------|-------------------------|\n| **1. Request Initiation** | Student/Admin triggers TC request | Requires valid reason: College transfer, course withdrawal, completion |\n| **2. Clearance Checklist** | Auto-validates: Library dues, Lab clearance, Hostel/Transport (if applicable), Fee status | Financial hold **CAN** block TC issuance (permissible under UGC) |\n| **3. Original Document Surrender** | Admin uploads verification: Original TC/LC from previous institution, marksheets, ID proof | System logs receipt date, admin signature, document serial numbers |\n| **4. TC Generation** | PDF generated with unique serial, QR code, digital signature placeholder, issuance date | Anti-forgery: QR links to public verification portal |\n| **5. Physical Issuance Log** | Track: Printed → Handed over → Student signature collected → Date/Time | Prevents \"ghost\" certificates; audit-ready |\n| **6. Status Lock** | Student status → `TRANSFERRED` or `WITHDRAWN` | Blocks further academic activity in current college |\n\n### B. Degree Certificate Generation (Autonomous Colleges)\n\n| Stage | System Action | Compliance/Verification |\n|-------|---------------|-------------------------|\n| **1. Eligibility Check** | Final year cleared, zero backlogs, attendance met, ordinance compliant | Auto-flags if ATKT backlogs remain |\n| **2. Fee & Clearance** | Financial clearance verified; degree issuance can be held for pending fees | UGC-compliant: progression allowed, degree release blocked |\n| **3. Template Selection** | Choose from college-configured degree templates (Autonomous vs Affiliated) | Supports bilingual (English + Regional), university crest, convocation details |\n| **4. Batch Generation** | Convocation-ready batch export, serial numbering, watermark, QR verification | Matches UGC/AICTE degree format standards |\n| **5. Physical Issuance & Registry** | Log: Printed → Distributed → Recipient signature → Date | Degree registry export for university affiliation compliance |\n| **6. Public Verification** | QR code links to `verify.novaa.edu/degree/{serial}` | Prevents fake degree circulation; employer/university verification |\n\n### Anti-Double-Enrollment Safeguards\n1. **Status Locking**: `ACTIVE` → `TRANSFERRED`/`GRADUATED`/`WITHDRAWN`. System blocks re-enrollment in same college without status reset.\n2. **Original Surrender Mandate**: TC generation requires admin confirmation that original previous-college TC was physically collected.\n3. **Unique Student Identifier**: Maps to University/State roll number; flags duplicate active enrollments across tenants (if integrated with state portal in future).\n4. **Audit Trail**: Every TC/Degree issuance logs `issued_to`, `issued_by`, `original_docs_received`, `ip`, `timestamp`. Fraudulent issuance is traceable.\n\n---\n\n## 🔗 Integration & Cross-Module Workflow\n\n```\nMarks Entry → Ordinance Calculation → Results Published\n       ↓\nAcademic Status Update (PASSED / ATKT / DETAINED)\n       ↓\nClearance Checks (Library, Lab, Fees, Original Docs)\n       ↓\nCertificate Eligibility → LC/TC or Degree Generation\n       ↓\nPhysical Issuance Logging → Status Lock → Public Verification QR\n       ↓\nAudit Log + DPDPA Retention Policy Applied\n```\n\n> ⚠️ **Critical Compliance Note**:  \n> - **Promotion/Exam Eligibility** → Cannot be blocked for fee dues (UGC mandate)  \n> - **TC/Degree Issuance** → CAN be held for fee dues, original document surrender, or disciplinary action  \n> - System enforces this separation via `academic_status` vs `document_release_status` flags\n\n---\n\n## ✅ PRD Acceptance Criteria\n\n| Feature | Validation Method |\n|---------|------------------|\n| Ordinance engine applies rules per college config | Test with Mumbai Univ vs Pune Univ templates; verify different outcomes |\n| Grace/roundoff applied pre-pass/fail | Input 39.4, 39.5, 38 marks; verify pass status matches ordinance |\n| ATKT limit enforces conditional promotion | Config limit=2; test with 1, 2, 3 backlogs; verify outcomes |\n| Financial hold blocks TC/Degree but not promotion | Test with pending fees; verify student advances but certificate status = HELD |\n| Original document surrender logged before TC generation | Admin must check \"Originals Received\" + upload proof; system blocks generation otherwise |\n| QR verification works for TC & Degree | Scan QR → redirects to public verification page with serial, student name, issue date, college seal |\n| Status lock prevents dual enrollment | Attempt re-admission with same roll number → system blocks with \"Already transferred/graduated\" |\n| Batch degree generation for autonomous colleges | Select convocation year → generates 50+ degrees with sequential serials, watermarks, QR codes |\n| Manual result override requires audit | Override flow captures justification, approver, timestamp; logs in audit trail |\n| DPDPA data retention applied | Degree/LC/TC records retained 10 years; auto-archive after retention period with anonymization |\n\n---\n\n## 📅 MVP vs V1.1 Scope\n\n| Feature | MVP | V1.1 |\n|--------|-----|------|\n| Marks entry + ordinance calculation | ✅ | Advanced grade capping rules |\n| Result publication + transcript PDF | ✅ | Digital signature integration |\n| LC/TC generation + issuance log | ✅ | Inter-college status verification API |\n| Degree template engine (Autonomous) | ✅ | Bulk convocation dispatch workflow |\n| Financial hold on certificate release | ✅ | Partial fee release + installment-based certificate unlock |\n| Anti-double-enrollment status lock | ✅ | State university roll-number sync |\n| Original document surrender checklist | ✅ | OCR validation of surrendered documents |\n| Public QR verification portal | ✅ | Blockchain-backed verification (optional) |\n\n---\n\n## 🛡️ Compliance & Risk Mitigation\n\n| Risk | Mitigation |\n|------|------------|\n| **Fake TC/Degree circulation** | QR verification, unique serials, public validation portal, admin issuance audit |\n| **UGC non-compliance (fee blocks)** | Strict separation: `academic_status` ≠ `document_release_status`; system enforces UGC rule |\n| **Data loss during certificate generation** | Version-controlled templates, backup PDF storage, audit trail for every generation |\n| **Manual override abuse** | Cap to 1/cycle, mandatory justification, Principal/HOD dual approval, IP + timestamp logging |\n| **Double enrollment fraud** | Status locking, original surrender mandate, roll-number uniqueness, future state portal integration |\n| **DPDPA exposure** | Explicit consent for certificate data, 10-year retention policy, anonymization post-retention |\n\n---\n\n## 📌 PRD Integration Guidance\n\n1. **Add** `Examination & Results Processing` and `Certificate Management` as standalone modules in your PRD feature matrix.\n2. **Link** them to the existing `Student Promotion` module (now renamed `Academic Progression Engine`).\n3. **Flag** UGC compliance notes for legal review before pilot launch.\n4. **Use** acceptance criteria directly for QA test case generation.\n5. **Prioritize** MVP scope: Results engine → TC/LC generation → Degree templates → QR verification.\n\n> 💡 **Implementation Tip**: Start with **TC/LC workflow first** — it's the highest manual-to-digital pain point for Indian colleges.
